import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { 
  Shield, Users, Heart, Crosshair, Search, Brain, Wrench, 
  Ghost, Save, Bomb, Dog, Trash2, Info, LayoutGrid, Lock, AlertTriangle, KeyRound, Square, CheckSquare 
} from 'lucide-react';
import type { CharacterSheet, TeamRole } from '../../types/characterSchema';
import { TEAM_ROLES, type TeamAbility } from '../../data/teamPowers';
import { CLASS_POWERS, type ClassPower } from '../../data/classPowers';
import { SKILL_LIST } from '../../data/referenceData';

interface Props {
  character: CharacterSheet;
  onUpdate: (updates: any) => void;
}

const ICONS: Record<string, any> = {
  tanque: Shield, suporte: Users, curandeiro: Heart, oportunista: Crosshair,
  investigador: Search, terapeuta: Brain, sabotador: Bomb, polivalente: Wrench, lobo_solitario: Dog
};

const SHAPE_STYLES: Record<number, string> = {
  1: 'rounded-full',
  2: 'rounded-full',
  3: 'rounded-full',
  4: 'rounded-full',
  5: 'rounded-md'
};

const ACTIVE_COLORS = {
  1: 'bg-blue-500 text-white shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(59,130,246,0.5)] scale-110',
  2: 'bg-cyan-500 text-white shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(6,182,212,0.5)] scale-110',
  3: 'bg-violet-500 text-white shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(139,92,246,0.5)] scale-110',
  4: 'bg-fuchsia-500 text-white shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(217,70,239,0.5)] scale-110',
  5: 'bg-rose-600 text-white shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(244,63,94,0.5)] scale-110'
};

const INACTIVE_STYLE = 'bg-eden-900/40 text-eden-100/10 border border-eden-700/30 hover:border-eden-500 cursor-pointer';
const ROMAN_NUMERALS = { 1: 'I', 2: 'II', 3: 'III', 4: 'IV', 5: 'V' };

export default function SheetTeam({ character, onUpdate }: Props) {
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<'role' | 'formation' | 'selector'>('role');
  
  // Estados para Lobo Solitário
  const [selectedClassPowerId, setSelectedClassPowerId] = useState<string>('');
  const [selectedSkills, setSelectedSkills] = useState<string[]>([]);
  
  // Estados para Formação
  const [currentFormation, setCurrentFormation] = useState<(string | null)[]>(Array(25).fill(null));
  const [selectedTool, setSelectedTool] = useState<'C' | 'E' | 'O' | 'X'>('C');
  
  // Info Hover
  const [hoveredInfo, setHoveredInfo] = useState<{ title: string, desc: string, level?: string } | null>(null);

  // Estados de Segurança (Senha)
  const [showPasswordModal, setShowPasswordModal] = useState(false);
  const [passwordInput, setPasswordInput] = useState('');

  // Carregar formação salva
  useEffect(() => {
    if (character.teamStrategy.favoriteFormations && character.teamStrategy.favoriteFormations[0]) {
        const saved = character.teamStrategy.favoriteFormations[0].split(',');
        const parsed = saved.map(s => s === '' ? null : s);
        if (parsed.length === 25) setCurrentFormation(parsed);
    }
  }, []);

  const updateTeamStrategy = (updates: Partial<typeof character.teamStrategy>) => {
    onUpdate({
        teamStrategy: {
            ...character.teamStrategy,
            ...updates
        }
    });
  };

  // --- LÓGICA DE PONTOS E LIMITES ---
  const getMaxAbilityPoints = () => {
      return Math.floor((character.progression.nex + 5) / 10);
  };

  const getCurrentPointsUsed = () => {
      return character.teamStrategy.roleAbilities.reduce((acc, ab) => acc + ab.currentLevel, 0);
  };

  // --- LÓGICA DE FUNÇÃO ---
  const handleRoleSelect = (roleId: string) => {
    if (confirm("ATENÇÃO: Mudar de função resetará todas as suas habilidades de equipe atuais. Deseja continuar?")) {
        updateTeamStrategy({ role: roleId as TeamRole, roleAbilities: [] });
        setSelectedClassPowerId('');
        setSelectedSkills([]);
        setActiveTab('role');
        setShowPasswordModal(false);
        setPasswordInput('');
    }
  };

  const handleAbilityChange = (abilityId: string, abilityName: string, newLevel: number) => {
    const currentAbilities = [...character.teamStrategy.roleAbilities];
    const existingIndex = currentAbilities.findIndex(a => a.id === abilityId);
    const currentLevel = existingIndex !== -1 ? currentAbilities[existingIndex].currentLevel : 0;

    if (newLevel > currentLevel) {
        const pointsUsed = getCurrentPointsUsed();
        const maxPoints = getMaxAbilityPoints();
        const cost = newLevel - currentLevel;

        if (pointsUsed + cost > maxPoints) {
            alert(`Limite de pontos atingido! Você tem ${pointsUsed}/${maxPoints} níveis alocados (Baseado em NEX ${character.progression.nex}%).`);
            return;
        }
    }

    if (newLevel === 0) {
        if (existingIndex !== -1) currentAbilities.splice(existingIndex, 1);
    } else {
        if (existingIndex !== -1) {
            currentAbilities[existingIndex].currentLevel = newLevel as any;
        } else {
            currentAbilities.push({ id: abilityId, name: abilityName, currentLevel: newLevel as any });
        }
    }
    updateTeamStrategy({ roleAbilities: currentAbilities });
  };

  // --- SEGURANÇA / SENHA ---
  const handleUnlockSelector = () => {
      const date = new Date();
      const day = date.getDate();
      const month = date.getMonth() + 1; 
      const year = date.getFullYear();
      
      const magicNumber = day + month + year;
      console.log("Senha Esperada (Dia+Mês+Ano):", magicNumber);

      if (passwordInput === magicNumber.toString()) {
          setActiveTab('selector');
          setShowPasswordModal(false);
          setPasswordInput('');
      } else {
          alert("Código de acesso incorreto. Acesso negado.");
      }
  };

  // --- LÓGICA LOBO SOLITÁRIO ---
  const availableClassPowers = CLASS_POWERS.filter((p: ClassPower) => 
    (p.class === character.progression.class || p.class === 'all') && p.id !== 'transcender'
  );

  const addLoneWolfPower = () => {
      if (!selectedClassPowerId) return;
      const power = CLASS_POWERS.find(p => p.id === selectedClassPowerId);
      if (!power) return;
      
      if (power.needsSelection === 'skills' && selectedSkills.length !== 2) {
          alert("Selecione exatamente 2 perícias.");
          return;
      }

      const newPowerEntry = {
          nexSource: character.progression.nex,
          powerId: power.id,
          powerName: power.name + (selectedSkills.length ? ` (${selectedSkills.join(', ')})` : '')
      };

      updateTeamStrategy({
          loneWolf: {
              ...character.teamStrategy.loneWolf,
              isActive: true,
              extraPowersChosen: [...character.teamStrategy.loneWolf.extraPowersChosen, newPowerEntry]
          }
      });
      
      setSelectedClassPowerId('');
      setSelectedSkills([]);
  };

  const removeLoneWolfPower = (index: number) => {
      const newPowers = [...character.teamStrategy.loneWolf.extraPowersChosen];
      newPowers.splice(index, 1);
      updateTeamStrategy({
          loneWolf: { ...character.teamStrategy.loneWolf, extraPowersChosen: newPowers }
      });
  };

  // --- LÓGICA DE FORMAÇÃO ---
  const handleGridClick = (index: number) => {
    const newGrid = [...currentFormation];
    if (selectedTool === 'X') newGrid[index] = null;
    else newGrid[index] = selectedTool;
    setCurrentFormation(newGrid);
  };

  const saveFormation = (slot: 1 | 2) => {
    const formationString = currentFormation.map(c => c || '').join(',');
    const newFavs = [...(character.teamStrategy.favoriteFormations || [])];
    while(newFavs.length < 2) newFavs.push(""); 
    
    if (slot === 1) newFavs[0] = formationString;
    else newFavs[1] = formationString;

    updateTeamStrategy({ favoriteFormations: newFavs });
    alert(`Formação salva no Slot ${slot}!`);
  };

  const loadFormation = (slot: 1 | 2) => {
      const favs = character.teamStrategy.favoriteFormations || [];
      const target = slot === 1 ? favs[0] : favs[1];
      
      if (!target) {
          alert("Slot vazio.");
          return;
      }

      const parsed = target.split(',').map(s => s === '' ? null : s);
      if (parsed.length === 25) setCurrentFormation(parsed);
  };

  const toggleFormationActive = () => {
      updateTeamStrategy({ isFormationActive: !character.teamStrategy.isFormationActive });
  };

  const currentRoleData = TEAM_ROLES.find(r => r.id === character.teamStrategy.role);
  const RoleIcon = currentRoleData ? (ICONS[currentRoleData.id] || Shield) : Shield;
  const isLoneWolf = character.teamStrategy.role === 'lobo_solitario';

  return (
    <div className="h-full flex flex-col animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-bottom-4">
      
      {/* SUB-HEADER DE NAVEGAÇÃO */}
      <div className="flex justify-center gap-4 mb-6">
        <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('role')} className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-6 py-2 rounded-full font-bold transition-all ${activeTab === 'role' ? 'bg-energia text-eden-900' : 'bg-eden-800 text-eden-100 border border-eden-700'}`}>
            <Users size={16}/> Habilidades
        </button>
        <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('formation')} className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-6 py-2 rounded-full font-bold transition-all ${activeTab === 'formation' ? 'bg-conhecimento text-eden-900' : 'bg-eden-800 text-eden-100 border border-eden-700'}`}>
            <LayoutGrid size={16}/> Formação
        </button>
        <button onClick={() => setShowPasswordModal(true)} className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-6 py-2 rounded-full font-bold transition-all ${activeTab === 'selector' ? 'bg-red-500 text-white' : 'bg-eden-900/50 text-eden-100/50 border border-eden-700 hover:text-red-400 hover:border-red-500/50'}`}>
            <Lock size={14}/> Alterar Função
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* MODAL DE SENHA */}
      {showPasswordModal && (
          <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/90 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-[90] p-4 animate-in zoom-in-95">
              <div className="bg-eden-900 border border-red-500/50 rounded-2xl w-full max-w-md p-6 shadow-2xl">
                  <div className="text-center mb-6">
                      <div className="w-16 h-16 bg-red-900/20 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center mx-auto mb-4 border-2 border-red-500">
                          <Lock size={32} className="text-red-500" />
                      </div>
                      <h3 className="text-2xl font-black text-eden-100 mb-2">Área Restrita</h3>
                      <div className="p-4 bg-red-950/30 border border-red-900/50 rounded-lg text-left">
                          <p className="text-sm text-red-200/80 flex gap-3 items-start">
                              <AlertTriangle className="shrink-0 mt-0.5" size={16}/>
                              <span>
                                  <strong>Atenção Agente:</strong> Esta área permite alterar sua Função Tática. Isso deve ser feito apenas se você escolheu a função errada durante a criação da ficha E com autorização expressa do Mestre, o qual irá lhe passar a senha.
                              </span>
                          </p>
                      </div>
                  </div>
                  
                  <div className="space-y-4">
                      <div>
                          <label className="text-xs font-bold text-eden-100/50 uppercase mb-1 block">Código de Autorização</label>
                          <div className="relative">
                              <KeyRound className="absolute left-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-eden-100/30" size={16} />
                              <input 
                                  type="number" 
                                  autoFocus
                                  value={passwordInput}
                                  onChange={(e) => setPasswordInput(e.target.value)}
                                  onKeyDown={(e) => e.key === 'Enter' && handleUnlockSelector()}
                                  className="w-full bg-eden-950 border border-eden-700 rounded-lg py-3 pl-10 text-eden-100 outline-none focus:border-red-500 font-mono text-center tracking-widest text-lg"
                                  placeholder="0000"
                                  style={{ colorScheme: 'dark' }}
                              />
                          </div>
                      </div>
                      <div className="flex gap-3">
                          <button onClick={() => { setShowPasswordModal(false); setPasswordInput(''); }} className="flex-1 py-3 rounded-lg font-bold text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-800 transition-colors">Cancelar</button>
                          <button onClick={handleUnlockSelector} className="flex-1 py-3 rounded-lg font-bold bg-red-600 text-white hover:bg-red-500 transition-colors shadow-lg">Acessar</button>
                      </div>
                  </div>
              </div>
          </div>
      )}

      {/* CONTEÚDO DA ABA FUNÇÃO (ÁRVORE) */}
      {activeTab === 'role' && (
        <div className="flex flex-col h-full">
            <div className="bg-eden-800 border border-eden-700 rounded-xl p-6 flex flex-col h-full relative">
                {currentRoleData ? (
                    <>
                        <div className="flex items-start gap-4 mb-6 border-b border-eden-700 pb-4 shrink-0">
                            <div className="p-4 bg-eden-900 rounded-2xl border border-eden-600">
                                <RoleIcon size={40} className="text-energia" />
                            </div>
                            <div className="flex-1">
                                <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                                    <h2 className="text-3xl font-black text-eden-100">{currentRoleData.name}</h2>
                                    {!isLoneWolf && (
                                        <div className="text-right">
                                            <div className="text-[10px] text-eden-100/40 uppercase font-bold">Pontos de Habilidade</div>
                                            <div className={`text-xl font-black ${getCurrentPointsUsed() >= getMaxAbilityPoints() ? 'text-red-500' : 'text-energia'}`}>
                                                {getCurrentPointsUsed()} / {getMaxAbilityPoints()}
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    )}
                                </div>
                                <p className="text-eden-100/70 text-sm mt-1 leading-relaxed">{currentRoleData.description}</p>
                            </div>
                        </div>

                        {isLoneWolf ? (
                            <div className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar space-y-6 pr-2">
                                <div className="p-4 bg-red-900/20 border border-red-500/50 rounded-xl text-red-200">
                                    <h3 className="font-bold mb-2 flex items-center gap-2"><Ghost size={18}/> Passiva: Caminho Solitário</h3>
                                    <p className="text-sm leading-relaxed">{currentRoleData.passive}</p>
                                </div>

                                {character.teamStrategy.loneWolf.extraPowersChosen.length > 0 && (
                                    <div className="space-y-2">
                                        <h4 className="text-xs font-bold uppercase text-eden-100/50">Poderes Adquiridos</h4>
                                        {character.teamStrategy.loneWolf.extraPowersChosen.map((p, idx) => (
                                            <div key={idx} className="flex justify-between items-center bg-eden-900/50 p-3 rounded border border-eden-700">
                                                <span className="text-sm font-bold text-eden-100">{p.powerName}</span>
                                                <button onClick={() => removeLoneWolfPower(idx)} className="text-red-500 hover:text-red-400"><Trash2 size={16}/></button>
                                            </div>
                                        ))}
                                    </div>
                                )}

                                <div className="bg-eden-900/30 p-4 rounded-xl border border-eden-700">
                                    <h3 className="font-bold text-eden-100 mb-3 text-sm">Adicionar Poder de Classe</h3>
                                    <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4">
                                        <select 
                                            value={selectedClassPowerId} 
                                            onChange={e => setSelectedClassPowerId(e.target.value)} 
                                            className="flex-1 bg-eden-950 border border-eden-600 rounded-lg p-2 text-sm text-eden-100 outline-none"
                                        >
                                            <option value="">Selecione...</option>
                                            {availableClassPowers.map(p => (
                                                <option key={p.id} value={p.id}>{p.name}</option>
                                            ))}
                                        </select>
                                        <button onClick={addLoneWolfPower} disabled={!selectedClassPowerId} className="px-4 bg-energia text-eden-900 font-bold rounded-lg text-xs hover:bg-yellow-400 disabled:opacity-50">
                                            Adicionar
                                        </button>
                                    </div>
                                    
                                    {selectedClassPowerId && CLASS_POWERS.find(p => p.id === selectedClassPowerId)?.needsSelection === 'skills' && (
                                        <div className="p-3 bg-eden-950 rounded border border-conhecimento/30 animate-in fade-in">
                                            <div className="text-xs text-conhecimento font-bold mb-2">Selecione 2 Perícias:</div>
                                            <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-2 max-h-32 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar">
                                                {SKILL_LIST.map(s => (
                                                    <button 
                                                        key={s} 
                                                        onClick={() => {
                                                            if (selectedSkills.includes(s)) setSelectedSkills(prev => prev.filter(sk => sk !== s));
                                                            else if (selectedSkills.length < 2) setSelectedSkills(prev => [...prev, s]);
                                                        }}
                                                        className={`text-[10px] p-1 rounded border ${selectedSkills.includes(s) ? 'bg-conhecimento text-eden-900 border-conhecimento' : 'border-eden-700 text-eden-100/50'}`}
                                                    >
                                                        {s}
                                                    </button>
                                                ))}
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    )}
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        ) : (
                            <div className="flex-1 flex flex-col min-h-0">
                                <div className="flex-1 grid grid-cols-4 gap-6 items-start p-4">
                                    {currentRoleData.abilities?.map((ability: TeamAbility) => {
                                        const userAbility = character.teamStrategy.roleAbilities.find(a => a.id === ability.id);
                                        const currentLevel = userAbility ? userAbility.currentLevel : 0;

                                        return (
                                            <div key={ability.id} className="flex flex-col items-center relative group h-full">
                                                <div className={`text-center text-xs font-bold mb-6 h-10 flex items-center justify-center border-b-2 w-full pb-2 ${currentLevel > 0 ? 'text-energia border-energia' : 'text-eden-100/50 border-eden-700/50'}`}>
                                                    {ability.name}
                                                </div>

                                                <div className="absolute top-16 bottom-4 w-0.5 bg-eden-700/30 -z-0 rounded-full" />

                                                <div className="flex flex-col justify-between h-full w-full py-2 z-10 items-center gap-4">
                                                    {[1, 2, 3, 4, 5].map((level) => {
                                                        const isUnlocked = currentLevel >= level;
                                                        let shapeClass = SHAPE_STYLES[level as keyof typeof SHAPE_STYLES] + ' w-12 h-12 flex items-center justify-center font-bold font-mono text-sm transition-all duration-300 shadow-sm ';
                                                        
                                                        if (isUnlocked) {
                                                            shapeClass += ACTIVE_COLORS[level as keyof typeof ACTIVE_COLORS] + ' z-20';
                                                        } else {
                                                            shapeClass += INACTIVE_STYLE;
                                                        }

                                                        return (
                                                            <button
                                                                key={level}
                                                                onClick={() => handleAbilityChange(ability.id, ability.name, currentLevel === level ? level - 1 : level)}
                                                                onMouseEnter={() => setHoveredInfo({ title: ability.name, level: `Nível ${ROMAN_NUMERALS[level as keyof typeof ROMAN_NUMERALS]}`, desc: ability.levels[level] })}
                                                                onMouseLeave={() => setHoveredInfo(null)}
                                                                className={shapeClass}
                                                            >
                                                                {ROMAN_NUMERALS[level as keyof typeof ROMAN_NUMERALS]}
                                                            </button>
                                                        );
                                                    })}
                                                </div>
                                            </div>
                                        );
                                    })}
                                </div>

                                <div className="mt-6 shrink-0 min-h-[120px] bg-eden-900/80 border border-eden-700 rounded-xl p-5 transition-all shadow-lg">
                                    {hoveredInfo ? (
                                        <div className="animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-bottom-1">
                                            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2 text-energia border-b border-eden-700/50 pb-2">
                                                <Info size={18} />
                                                <h4 className="font-bold text-sm uppercase tracking-wider">
                                                    {hoveredInfo.title} <span className="text-eden-100/50 ml-2 text-xs normal-case font-mono border border-eden-700 px-2 py-0.5 rounded bg-black/20">{hoveredInfo.level}</span>
                                                </h4>
                                            </div>
                                            <p className="text-sm text-eden-100/90 leading-relaxed">{hoveredInfo.desc}</p>
                                        </div>
                                    ) : (
                                        <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-eden-100/30 text-xs italic">
                                            Passe o mouse sobre um nível para ver os detalhes.
                                        </div>
                                    )}
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        )}
                    </>
                ) : (
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full text-eden-100/30 flex-col gap-4">
                        <Shield size={64} strokeWidth={1}/>
                        <p>Nenhuma função selecionada. Vá em "Alterar Função".</p>
                    </div>
                )}
            </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* CONTEÚDO DA ABA SELETOR (PROTEGIDA) */}
      {activeTab === 'selector' && (
          <div className="bg-eden-800/50 border border-eden-700 rounded-xl p-4 h-full overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar">
              <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-4 border-b border-eden-700 pb-4">
                  <div>
                      <h3 className="text-xl font-bold text-eden-100">Seletor de Função</h3>
                      <p className="text-xs text-eden-100/50">Escolha com sabedoria. Esta ação redefine sua estratégia.</p>
                  </div>
                  <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('role')} className="text-sm text-eden-100/50 hover:text-white underline">Voltar</button>
              </div>
              <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                {TEAM_ROLES.map(role => {
                    const Icon = ICONS[role.id] || Shield;
                    const isSelected = character.teamStrategy.role === role.id;
                    return (
                        <button key={role.id} onClick={() => !isSelected && handleRoleSelect(role.id)} className={`text-left p-4 rounded-xl border flex flex-col gap-3 transition-all hover:scale-[1.02] ${isSelected ? 'bg-energia/20 border-energia text-eden-100 ring-1 ring-energia' : 'bg-eden-900/50 border-eden-700 hover:bg-eden-800'}`}>
                            <div className="flex justify-between items-start">
                                <div className={`p-3 rounded-xl bg-eden-950 ${isSelected ? 'text-energia' : 'text-eden-100/50'}`}><Icon size={24} /></div>
                                {isSelected && <span className="text-[10px] bg-energia text-eden-900 px-2 py-1 rounded font-bold uppercase">Atual</span>}
                            </div>
                            <div>
                                <div className={`font-bold text-lg ${isSelected ? 'text-white' : 'text-eden-100/80'}`}>{role.name}</div>
                                <div className="text-xs text-eden-100/40 mt-1 leading-relaxed">{role.description}</div>
                            </div>
                        </button>
                    )
                })}
              </div>
          </div>
      )}

      {/* CONTEÚDO DA ABA FORMAÇÃO */}
      {activeTab === 'formation' && (
        <div className="flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-8 h-auto items-start justify-center p-4">
            
            {/* Ferramentas */}
            <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 bg-eden-800 p-6 rounded-xl border border-eden-700 w-full max-w-xs shadow-xl self-start sticky top-4">
                <h3 className="font-bold text-eden-100 text-center mb-2 flex items-center justify-center gap-2"><Wrench size={16}/> Ferramentas</h3>
                <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-2">
                    <button onClick={() => setSelectedTool('C')} className={`p-3 rounded-lg border flex items-center gap-2 transition-all ${selectedTool === 'C' ? 'bg-red-500/20 border-red-500 text-white' : 'bg-eden-900/50 border-eden-700 text-eden-100/50'}`}>
                        <div className="w-6 h-6 bg-red-600 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-bold shadow">C</div> Combat
                    </button>
                    <button onClick={() => setSelectedTool('E')} className={`p-3 rounded-lg border flex items-center gap-2 transition-all ${selectedTool === 'E' ? 'bg-emerald-500/20 border-emerald-500 text-white' : 'bg-eden-900/50 border-eden-700 text-eden-100/50'}`}>
                        <div className="w-6 h-6 bg-emerald-600 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-bold shadow">E</div> Espec
                    </button>
                    <button onClick={() => setSelectedTool('O')} className={`p-3 rounded-lg border flex items-center gap-2 transition-all ${selectedTool === 'O' ? 'bg-violet-500/20 border-violet-500 text-white' : 'bg-eden-900/50 border-eden-700 text-eden-100/50'}`}>
                        <div className="w-6 h-6 bg-violet-600 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-xs font-bold shadow">O</div> Ocult
                    </button>
                    <button onClick={() => setSelectedTool('X')} className={`p-3 rounded-lg border flex items-center gap-2 transition-all ${selectedTool === 'X' ? 'bg-eden-100/20 border-eden-100 text-white' : 'bg-eden-900/50 border-eden-700 text-eden-100/50'}`}>
                        <Trash2 size={18} /> Apagar
                    </button>
                </div>

                <div className="h-px bg-eden-700 my-2"></div>

                <div className="space-y-3">
                    <div className="flex gap-2">
                        <button onClick={() => saveFormation(1)} className="flex-1 py-2 bg-eden-900 hover:bg-eden-700 border border-eden-600 rounded text-xs font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-1"><Save size={12}/> Salvar 1</button>
                        <button onClick={() => loadFormation(1)} className="flex-1 py-2 bg-eden-900 hover:bg-eden-700 border border-eden-600 rounded text-xs font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-1">Carregar 1</button>
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex gap-2">
                        <button onClick={() => saveFormation(2)} className="flex-1 py-2 bg-eden-900 hover:bg-eden-700 border border-eden-600 rounded text-xs font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-1"><Save size={12}/> Salvar 2</button>
                        <button onClick={() => loadFormation(2)} className="flex-1 py-2 bg-eden-900 hover:bg-eden-700 border border-eden-600 rounded text-xs font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-1">Carregar 2</button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            {/* GRID 5x5 e REGRAS */}
            <div className="flex flex-col gap-4 w-full max-w-md">
                {/* Bloco de Regras da Formação */}
                <div className="bg-conhecimento/10 border border-conhecimento/30 rounded-xl p-4 text-sm text-eden-100/90 leading-relaxed shadow-lg">
                    <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2 text-conhecimento font-bold uppercase text-xs tracking-wider">
                        <Info size={14} /> Bônus de Formação
                    </div>
                    <p>
                        Se, durante uma cena, a equipe estiver nas exatas posições marcadas no grid, todos na formação recebem:
                    </p>
                    <ul className="mt-2 space-y-1 text-xs font-bold text-white list-disc pl-4">
                        <li>+2 em quaisquer testes</li>
                        <li>+1 em rolagens de dano</li>
                        <li>+1 na Defesa</li>
                    </ul>
                </div>

                <div className="relative p-8 bg-eden-900/50 rounded-2xl border border-eden-700 shadow-2xl">
                    <div className="grid grid-cols-5 gap-2 pt-5">
                        {currentFormation.map((cell, index) => (
                            <div 
                                key={index} 
                                onClick={() => handleGridClick(index)} 
                                className="w-14 h-14 md:w-16 md:h-16 bg-eden-800 rounded-lg border border-eden-700 hover:border-eden-500 cursor-pointer flex items-center justify-center transition-all hover:scale-105 shadow-inner relative"
                            >
                                <div className="absolute inset-0 opacity-10 bg-[url('https://www.transparenttextures.com/patterns/hexellence.png')] pointer-events-none"></div>
                                {cell === 'C' && <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-red-600 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-white font-bold shadow-lg border-2 border-red-400">C</div>}
                                {cell === 'E' && <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-emerald-600 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-white font-bold shadow-lg border-2 border-emerald-400">E</div>}
                                {cell === 'O' && <div className="w-10 h-10 bg-violet-600 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-white font-bold shadow-lg border-2 border-violet-400">O</div>}
                            </div>
                        ))}
                    </div>
                    <div className="absolute -bottom-8 left-0 w-full text-center text-xs text-eden-100/30 font-mono uppercase tracking-widest">
                        Grid Tático 5x5 (1,5m/q)
                    </div>
                    
                    {/* CHECKBOX DE ATIVAÇÃO (Reposicionado: Topo Direito dentro do Card) */}
                    <div className="absolute top-3 right-3">
                         <button 
                             onClick={toggleFormationActive}
                             className={`flex items-center gap-2 text-xs font-bold px-2 py-1 rounded border transition-colors ${character.teamStrategy.isFormationActive ? 'text-conhecimento border-conhecimento/30 bg-conhecimento/10' : 'text-eden-100/30 border-transparent hover:text-white hover:bg-white/5'}`}
                         >
                             {character.teamStrategy.isFormationActive ? <CheckSquare size={14} /> : <Square size={14} />}
                             Bônus Ativo
                         </button>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

import { User, Scroll, Users, VenetianMask } from 'lucide-react';
import { useCharacter } from '../../context/CharacterContext';

export default function Step1Concept() {
  const { character, updateInfo } = useCharacter();

  return (
    <div className="space-y-6 animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-bottom-4 duration-500">
      <div className="text-center mb-8">
        <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold text-eden-100">Identidade do Agente</h2>
        <p className="text-eden-100/50">Quem você era antes de conhecer o Outro Lado?</p>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6">
        {/* Nome do Personagem */}
        <div className="space-y-2">
          <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-eden-100/70">
            <User className="w-4 h-4 text-energia" /> Nome do Personagem
          </label>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={character.info.name}
            onChange={(e) => updateInfo('name', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full bg-eden-900 border border-eden-700 rounded-lg p-3 text-eden-100 focus:border-energia focus:ring-1 focus:ring-energia outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-eden-700"
            placeholder="Ex: Arthur Cervero"
          />
        </div>

        {/* Jogador */}
        <div className="space-y-2">
          <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-eden-100/70">
            <Users className="w-4 h-4 text-conhecimento" /> Jogador
          </label>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={character.info.player}
            onChange={(e) => updateInfo('player', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full bg-eden-900 border border-eden-700 rounded-lg p-3 text-eden-100 focus:border-conhecimento focus:ring-1 focus:ring-conhecimento outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-eden-700"
            placeholder="Seu nome real"
          />
        </div>

        {/* Arquétipo / Conceito */}
        <div className="space-y-2 md:col-span-2">
          <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-eden-100/70">
            <VenetianMask className="w-4 h-4 text-sangue" /> Conceito
          </label>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={character.info.archetype}
            onChange={(e) => updateInfo('archetype', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full bg-eden-900 border border-eden-700 rounded-lg p-3 text-eden-100 focus:border-sangue focus:ring-1 focus:ring-sangue outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-eden-700"
            placeholder="Ex: Um ex-militar buscando vingança..."
          />
        </div>

        {/* Idade e Gênero */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
            <div className="space-y-2">
            <label className="text-sm font-medium text-eden-100/70">Idade</label>
            <input
                type="number"
                value={character.info.age || ''}
                onChange={(e) => updateInfo('age', parseInt(e.target.value))}
                className="w-full bg-eden-900 border border-eden-700 rounded-lg p-3 text-eden-100 focus:border-eden-100 outline-none transition-all"
            />
            </div>
            <div className="space-y-2">
            <label className="text-sm font-medium text-eden-100/70">Gênero</label>
            <input
                type="text"
                value={character.info.gender}
                onChange={(e) => updateInfo('gender', e.target.value)}
                className="w-full bg-eden-900 border border-eden-700 rounded-lg p-3 text-eden-100 focus:border-eden-100 outline-none transition-all"
            />
            </div>
        </div>
        
        {/* Campanha */}
         <div className="space-y-2">
          <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-eden-100/70">
            <Scroll className="w-4 h-4 text-morte" /> Campanha
          </label>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={character.info.campaign}
            onChange={(e) => updateInfo('campaign', e.target.value)}
            className="w-full bg-eden-900 border border-eden-700 rounded-lg p-3 text-eden-100 focus:border-morte focus:ring-1 focus:ring-morte outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-eden-700"
            placeholder="Nome da missão"
          />
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useState } from 'react';
import { Brain, Zap, Shield, Eye, BicepsFlexed, HelpCircle, Info } from 'lucide-react';
import { useCharacter } from '../../context/CharacterContext';
import type { AttributeKey } from '../../types/characterSchema';

// Cores e Descrições
const ATTRIBUTE_DETAILS = {
  agi: { 
    label: 'Agilidade', 
    icon: Zap, 
    color: 'text-yellow-400', 
    borderColor: 'border-yellow-400',
    bgGradient: 'from-yellow-400/20',
    desc: 'Define sua coordenação motora, velocidade de reação e destreza manual. Essencial para Furtividade, Pilotagem e Pontaria.' 
  },
  for: { 
    label: 'Força', 
    icon: BicepsFlexed, 
    color: 'text-red-500', 
    borderColor: 'border-red-500',
    bgGradient: 'from-red-500/20',
    desc: 'Determina sua potência muscular e capacidade física. Afeta o dano corpo a corpo, capacidade de carga e testes de Atletismo.' 
  },
  int: { 
    label: 'Intelecto', 
    icon: Brain, 
    color: 'text-blue-400', 
    borderColor: 'border-blue-400',
    bgGradient: 'from-blue-400/20',
    desc: 'Mede raciocínio, memória e educação. Define o número de pericias treinadas e a compreensão de rituais ocultistas.' 
  },
  pre: { 
    label: 'Presença', 
    icon: Eye, 
    color: 'text-purple-400', 
    borderColor: 'border-purple-400',
    bgGradient: 'from-purple-400/20',
    desc: 'Sua força de vontade e carisma. Define seus Pontos de Esforço (PE) iniciais e resistência contra efeitos mentais.' 
  },
  vig: { 
    label: 'Vigor', 
    icon: Shield, 
    color: 'text-green-500', 
    borderColor: 'border-green-500',
    bgGradient: 'from-green-500/20',
    desc: 'Saúde e resistência física. Define seus Pontos de Vida (PV) iniciais e sua capacidade de sobreviver a ferimentos.' 
  },
};

export default function Step2Attributes() {
  const { character, updateAttribute } = useCharacter();
  const { attributes } = character;
  
  // Estado para controlar qual card está ativo (Hover no PC, Click no Mobile)
  const [activeKey, setActiveKey] = useState<AttributeKey | null>(null);

  // Lógica de Pontos
  const currentSum = Object.values(attributes).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
  const pointsRemaining = 4 - (currentSum - 5);
  const zerosCount = Object.values(attributes).filter(v => v === 0).length;

  const handleChange = (e: React.MouseEvent, key: AttributeKey, delta: number) => {
    e.stopPropagation(); // Impede que clicar no botão ative o card
    const currentVal = attributes[key];
    const newVal = currentVal + delta;

    if (newVal < 0 || newVal > 3) return;
    if (delta > 0 && pointsRemaining <= 0) return;
    if (newVal === 0 && zerosCount >= 1 && currentVal !== 0) return; 

    updateAttribute(key, newVal);
  };

  const activeInfo = activeKey ? ATTRIBUTE_DETAILS[activeKey] : null;

  return (
    <div className="animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-right-8 duration-500 pb-20 lg:pb-0">
      
      {/* Cabeçalho e Contador */}
      <div className="text-center mb-8 space-y-4">
        <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold text-eden-100">Defina seus Atributos</h2>
        
        <div className={`inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-6 py-2 rounded-full border transition-colors duration-300 ${
          pointsRemaining === 0 
            ? 'bg-eden-900 border-green-500 text-green-400 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(34,197,94,0.3)]' 
            : 'bg-eden-800 border-eden-600 text-eden-100'
        }`}>
          <span className="text-2xl font-bold">{pointsRemaining}</span>
          <span className="text-xs uppercase tracking-widest opacity-70">Pontos Restantes</span>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Container Flex Responsivo: Coluna no Mobile, Linha no Desktop */}
      <div className="flex flex-col lg:flex-row gap-8 items-start">
        
        {/* ÁREA DOS ATRIBUTOS (Centralizada) */}
        <div className="flex-1 w-full">
          <div className="flex flex-wrap justify-center gap-4">
            {(Object.entries(ATTRIBUTE_DETAILS) as [AttributeKey, typeof ATTRIBUTE_DETAILS['agi']][]).map(([key, info]) => {
              const Icon = info.icon;
              const value = attributes[key];
              const isActive = activeKey === key;

              return (
                <div 
                  key={key}
                  // No desktop usa hover, no mobile usa click
                  onMouseEnter={() => setActiveKey(key)}
                  onClick={() => setActiveKey(key)}
                  className={`
                    relative w-full sm:w-40 p-4 rounded-xl border flex flex-col items-center transition-all duration-300 cursor-pointer
                    ${isActive 
                      ? `bg-eden-800 border-${info.borderColor.split('-')[1]} shadow-lg scale-105 z-10` 
                      : 'bg-eden-800/50 border-eden-700 hover:border-eden-600 hover:bg-eden-800'
                    }
                  `}
                  style={{ 
                    borderColor: isActive ? undefined : '',
                    boxShadow: isActive ? `0 0 20px -5px var(--tw-shadow-color)` : 'none'
                  }}
                >
                  {/* Ícone */}
                  <div className={`mb-2 p-3 rounded-full bg-eden-900/50 ${info.color}`}>
                    <Icon size={24} />
                  </div>
                  
                  <h3 className="font-bold text-eden-100 text-sm uppercase tracking-wider">{info.label}</h3>
                  
                  {/* Valor */}
                  <div className={`text-4xl font-black my-3 transition-colors duration-300 ${isActive ? info.color : 'text-eden-100'}`}>
                    {value}
                  </div>

                  {/* Controles */}
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 w-full justify-center z-20">
                    <button
                      onClick={(e) => handleChange(e, key, -1)}
                      disabled={value <= 0 || (value === 1 && zerosCount >= 1)}
                      className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-eden-900 hover:bg-eden-700 text-eden-100 disabled:opacity-20 disabled:cursor-not-allowed flex items-center justify-center pb-1 text-xl font-bold transition-colors"
                    >
                      -
                    </button>
                    <button
                      onClick={(e) => handleChange(e, key, 1)}
                      disabled={value >= 3 || pointsRemaining <= 0}
                      className="w-8 h-8 rounded-full bg-eden-100 text-eden-900 hover:bg-white disabled:bg-eden-700 disabled:text-eden-500 disabled:cursor-not-allowed flex items-center justify-center pb-1 text-xl font-bold transition-colors"
                    >
                      +
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              );
            })}
          </div>

          {/* Gráfico Rápido Mobile (Aparece embaixo dos atributos) */}
           <div className="mt-8 p-4 bg-eden-900/30 rounded-lg border border-eden-700/30 text-center lg:hidden">
             <p className="text-xs text-eden-100/40 uppercase">Toque em um atributo para ver detalhes</p>
           </div>
        </div>

        {/* PAINEL LATERAL (Detalhes) */}
        <div className="w-full lg:w-80 shrink-0">
          <div className={`sticky top-4 min-h-[200px] rounded-2xl border p-6 transition-all duration-500 flex flex-col items-center justify-center text-center relative overflow-hidden ${
            activeInfo 
              ? `bg-eden-800 border-${activeInfo.borderColor.split('-')[1]} shadow-xl` 
              : 'bg-eden-800/30 border-eden-700/50 border-dashed'
          }`}>
            
            {activeInfo ? (
              <div className="relative z-10 animate-in fade-in zoom-in-95 duration-300">
                <div className={`absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-b ${activeInfo.bgGradient} to-transparent opacity-20 -z-10 rounded-2xl blur-xl`} />
                
                <activeInfo.icon size={48} className={`mx-auto mb-4 ${activeInfo.color}`} />
                
                <h3 className={`text-2xl font-bold mb-3 ${activeInfo.color}`}>
                  {activeInfo.label}
                </h3>
                
                <p className="text-eden-100/80 text-sm leading-relaxed">
                  {activeInfo.desc}
                </p>

                <div className="mt-4 pt-4 border-t border-eden-100/10 text-xs text-eden-100/50 font-mono">
                  {activeInfo.label === 'Vigor' && <span>+{attributes.vig} PV / NEX</span>}
                  {activeInfo.label === 'Presença' && <span>+{attributes.pre} PE / NEX</span>}
                  {activeInfo.label === 'Intelecto' && <span>+{attributes.int} Perícias Extras</span>}
                  {activeInfo.label === 'Força' && <span>Carga: {attributes.for * 5 + (attributes.for === 0 ? 2 : 0)}</span>}
                  {activeInfo.label === 'Agilidade' && <span>Defesa Base: {10 + attributes.agi}</span>}
                </div>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="text-eden-100/20 flex flex-col items-center">
                <HelpCircle size={48} className="mb-4" />
                <p className="text-sm font-medium">Selecione um atributo</p>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* Resumo Geral (Aparece sempre no Desktop) */}
          <div className="hidden lg:block mt-6 p-4 bg-eden-900/50 rounded-xl border border-eden-700/50">
             <div className="text-xs text-eden-100/30 uppercase tracking-widest mb-3 flex items-center gap-2">
               <Info size={14} /> Status Base
             </div>
             <div className="space-y-2 text-sm text-eden-100/60">
                <div className="flex justify-between"><span>PV Inicial</span> <strong className="text-eden-100">{12 + attributes.vig} + Classe</strong></div>
                <div className="flex justify-between"><span>PE Inicial</span> <strong className="text-eden-100">{1 + attributes.pre} + Classe</strong></div>
                <div className="flex justify-between"><span>SAN Inicial</span> <strong className="text-eden-100">Classe</strong></div>
             </div>
          </div>
        </div>

      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: Step3Origins.tsx
PATH: D:\Programs\eden-arquivos\eden-arquivos\src\components\wizard\Step3Origins.tsx
========================================
import { useState } from 'react';
import { useCharacter } from '../../context/CharacterContext';
import { ORIGINS } from '../../data/origins';
import type { Origin } from '../../data/origins';
import { Search, BookOpen, Award, Bookmark } from 'lucide-react';

export default function Step3Origins() {
  const { character, updateProgression } = useCharacter();
  const [searchTerm, setSearchTerm] = useState('');
  
  // Inicializa com a origem já salva no contexto (se houver)
  const [selectedOrigin, setSelectedOrigin] = useState<Origin | null>(
    ORIGINS.find(o => o.name === character.progression.origin.name) || null
  );

  const filteredOrigins = ORIGINS.filter(origin => 
    origin.name.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase()) ||
    origin.skills.some(s => s.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase())) ||
    origin.source.toLowerCase().includes(searchTerm.toLowerCase())
  );

  const handleSelect = (origin: Origin) => {
    setSelectedOrigin(origin);
    
    // Atualiza a progressão
    updateProgression('origin', { id: origin.id, name: origin.name });
    
    // Opcional: Salvar no info como arquétipo/conceito
    // updateInfo('archetype', origin.name);
    
    // NOTA: A aplicação das perícias (treinamento) acontece automaticamente 
    // no Step4Classes ou SheetSkills através do useEffect que implementamos,
    // garantindo que se você trocar de origem, as perícias antigas não fiquem "presas".
  };

  const getSourceStyle = (source: string) => {
    if (source.includes('Livro')) {
      return 'bg-red-500/20 text-red-200 border-red-500/30 shadow-[0_0_10px_-5px_rgba(239,68,68,0.3)]';
    }
    if (source.includes('Sobrevivendo')) {
      return 'bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-200 border-blue-500/30 shadow-[0_0_10px_-5px_rgba(59,130,246,0.3)]';
    }
    if (source.includes('HQ')) {
      return 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-200 border-green-500/30 shadow-[0_0_10px_-5px_rgba(34,197,94,0.3)]';
    }
    return 'bg-eden-800 text-eden-100 border-eden-700';
  };

  return (
    <div className="h-[calc(100vh-200px)] flex flex-col gap-6 animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-right-8 duration-500">
      
      <div className="text-center space-y-2 shrink-0">
        <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold text-eden-100">Escolha sua Origem</h2>
        <p className="text-eden-100/50">O que você fazia antes de encarar o Paranormal?</p>
      </div>

      <div className="relative shrink-0">
        <Search className="absolute left-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 text-eden-100/40 w-5 h-5" />
        <input 
          type="text" 
          placeholder="Buscar por nome, perícia ou livro..."
          value={searchTerm}
          onChange={(e) => setSearchTerm(e.target.value)}
          className="w-full bg-eden-800 border border-eden-700 rounded-xl py-4 pl-12 pr-4 text-eden-100 focus:border-eden-100 focus:ring-1 focus:ring-eden-100 outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-eden-100/30"
        />
      </div>

      {/* Grid Principal com Overflow Hidden para conter o scroll */}
      <div className="flex-1 grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-2 gap-6 min-h-0 overflow-hidden">
        
        {/* Lista de Origens (Esquerda) - Scroll Independente */}
        <div className="space-y-3 overflow-y-auto pr-2 custom-scrollbar h-full">
          {filteredOrigins.map((origin) => (
            <button
              key={origin.id}
              onClick={() => handleSelect(origin)}
              className={`w-full text-left p-4 rounded-xl border transition-all duration-200 group relative overflow-hidden shrink-0 ${
                selectedOrigin?.id === origin.id
                  ? 'bg-eden-800 border-energia shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(124,58,237,0.2)]'
                  : 'bg-eden-800/30 border-eden-700 hover:border-eden-600 hover:bg-eden-800'
              }`}
            >
              <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-2 relative z-10 gap-4">
                <h3 className={`font-bold text-lg leading-tight line-clamp-2 break-words ${selectedOrigin?.id === origin.id ? 'text-energia' : 'text-eden-100'}`}>
                  {origin.name}
                </h3>
                {selectedOrigin?.id === origin.id && (
                  <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-energia animate-pulse shadow-[0_0_10px_#7c3aed] shrink-0 mt-1.5" />
                )}
              </div>
              
              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3 relative z-10">
                {origin.skills.map(skill => (
                  <span key={skill} className="text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded bg-eden-900/50 border border-eden-700/50 text-eden-100/70 group-hover:border-eden-500/50 transition-colors">
                    {skill}
                  </span>
                ))}
              </div>

              <div className="relative z-10">
                <span className={`inline-flex items-center gap-1 text-[10px] px-2 py-0.5 rounded border uppercase tracking-wider font-bold ${getSourceStyle(origin.source)}`}>
                  <Bookmark className="w-3 h-3" /> {origin.source}
                </span>
              </div>

              <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-r from-transparent via-white/[0.03] to-transparent -translate-x-full group-hover:translate-x-full transition-transform duration-1000 pointer-events-none" />
            </button>
          ))}
          
          {filteredOrigins.length === 0 && (
            <div className="text-center p-8 text-eden-100/30 italic border border-dashed border-eden-800 rounded-xl">
              Nenhuma origem encontrada.
            </div>
          )}
        </div>

        {/* Detalhes da Seleção (Direita) - Scroll Independente */}
        <div className="hidden lg:block h-full min-h-0">
          <div className={`h-full rounded-2xl border transition-all duration-500 relative overflow-hidden flex flex-col ${
             selectedOrigin 
               ? 'bg-eden-800 border-eden-600 shadow-2xl' 
               : 'bg-eden-800/10 border-eden-700/30 border-dashed items-center justify-center'
          }`}>
            {selectedOrigin ? (
              <div className="p-8 h-full overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar space-y-6 animate-in fade-in zoom-in-95 duration-300 relative z-10">
                <div>
                  <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-4">
                    <h3 className="text-4xl font-black text-eden-100">
                      {selectedOrigin.name}
                    </h3>
                  </div>
                  
                  <span className={`inline-block mb-4 text-xs px-3 py-1 rounded-full border ${getSourceStyle(selectedOrigin.source)} font-bold shadow-sm`}>
                    {selectedOrigin.source}
                  </span>

                  <p className="text-eden-100/80 leading-relaxed text-lg border-l-2 border-energia/50 pl-4 italic">
                    "{selectedOrigin.description}"
                  </p>
                </div>

                <div className="space-y-4">
                  <div className="p-5 bg-eden-900/50 rounded-xl border border-eden-700/50 hover:border-conhecimento/50 transition-colors group/card">
                    <h4 className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-bold text-conhecimento uppercase tracking-wider mb-3">
                      <BookOpen size={18} /> Perícias Treinadas
                    </h4>
                    <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                      {selectedOrigin.skills.length > 0 ? selectedOrigin.skills.map(skill => (
                        <span key={skill} className="px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg bg-eden-800 text-eden-100 text-sm font-medium border border-eden-700 shadow-sm">
                          {skill}
                        </span>
                      )) : (
                        <span className="text-eden-100/50 italic text-sm">À escolha do jogador (definido no próximo passo).</span>
                      )}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <div className="p-5 bg-eden-900/50 rounded-xl border border-eden-700/50 hover:border-sangue/50 transition-colors group/card">
                    <h4 className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-bold text-sangue uppercase tracking-wider mb-3">
                      <Award size={18} /> Poder: {selectedOrigin.power.name}
                    </h4>
                    <p className="text-sm text-eden-100/80 leading-relaxed">
                      {selectedOrigin.power.description}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            ) : (
              <div className="text-center text-eden-100/20">
                <Search size={64} className="mx-auto mb-6 opacity-30" />
                <p className="text-xl font-light">Selecione uma origem à esquerda</p>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>

      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

FILE: Step4Classes.tsx
PATH: D:\Programs\eden-arquivos\eden-arquivos\src\components\wizard\Step4Classes.tsx
========================================
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useCharacter } from '../../context/CharacterContext';
import { Sword, Book, Eye, Check, AlertTriangle, Pencil } from 'lucide-react';
import { SKILL_LIST } from '../../data/referenceData';
import { ORIGINS } from '../../data/origins';

export default function Step4Classes() {
  const { character, updateProgression } = useCharacter();
  
  // Inicializa com a classe salva ou null
  const [selectedClass, setSelectedClass] = useState<'combatente' | 'especialista' | 'ocultista' | null>(
    character.progression.class !== 'mundano' ? character.progression.class : null
  );

  const [combatenteFightChoice, setCombatenteFightChoice] = useState<'Luta' | 'Pontaria' | null>(null);
  const [combatenteResistChoice, setCombatenteResistChoice] = useState<'Fortitude' | 'Reflexos' | null>(null);
  const [selectedSkills, setSelectedSkills] = useState<string[]>([]);
  
  // Correção do aviso: ignorando a primeira variável do array
  const [, setForceUpdate] = useState(0); 

  // 1. Lógica de Origem
  const originName = character.progression.origin.name;
  const originData = ORIGINS.find(o => o.name === originName);
  const originSkills = originData?.skills || [];
  
  // Normaliza para garantir que "Profissão" bata com a lista
  const normalizedOriginSkills = originSkills.map(s => s === 'Profissão' ? 'Profissão' : s);

  // 2. Cálculo de Slots
  const calculateRequirements = () => {
      const int = character.attributes.int;
      let freeSlots = int;
      let needsFightChoice = false;
      let needsResistChoice = false;

      if (selectedClass === 'combatente') {
          const hasLuta = normalizedOriginSkills.includes('Luta');
          const hasPontaria = normalizedOriginSkills.includes('Pontaria');
          if (hasLuta || hasPontaria) freeSlots += 1; 
          else needsFightChoice = true;

          const hasFort = normalizedOriginSkills.includes('Fortitude');
          const hasRef = normalizedOriginSkills.includes('Reflexos');
          if (hasFort || hasRef) freeSlots += 1;
          else needsResistChoice = true;
          
          freeSlots += 1;
      } 
      else if (selectedClass === 'especialista') {
          freeSlots += 7;
      } 
      else if (selectedClass === 'ocultista') {
          if (normalizedOriginSkills.includes('Ocultismo')) freeSlots += 1;
          if (normalizedOriginSkills.includes('Vontade')) freeSlots += 1;
          freeSlots += 3;
      }
      return { freeSlots, needsFightChoice, needsResistChoice };
  };

  const { freeSlots, needsFightChoice, needsResistChoice } = calculateRequirements();

  // --- HANDLERS ---

  const handleClassSelect = (cls: 'combatente' | 'especialista' | 'ocultista') => {
    setSelectedClass(cls);
    setSelectedSkills([]);
    setCombatenteFightChoice(null);
    setCombatenteResistChoice(null);
    updateProgression('class', cls);
    
    // Reset de status base
    const statsMap = {
        combatente: { pv: 20, pe: 2, san: 12 },
        especialista: { pv: 16, pe: 3, san: 16 },
        ocultista: { pv: 12, pe: 4, san: 20 }
    };
    const stats = statsMap[cls];
    character.status.pv.max = stats.pv + character.attributes.vig;
    character.status.pv.current = character.status.pv.max;
    character.status.pe.max = stats.pe + character.attributes.pre;
    character.status.pe.current = character.status.pe.max;
    character.status.san.max = stats.san;
    character.status.san.current = stats.san;
  };

  const toggleSkill = (skill: string) => {
    // Se é da origem, não mexe
    if (normalizedOriginSkills.includes(skill)) return;
    
    // Se é automática de classe
    if (selectedClass === 'ocultista' && (skill === 'Ocultismo' || skill === 'Vontade')) return;

    if (selectedSkills.includes(skill)) {
      setSelectedSkills(prev => prev.filter(s => s !== skill));
    } else {
      if (selectedSkills.length < freeSlots) {
        setSelectedSkills(prev => [...prev, skill]);
      }
    }
  };

  const renameSkill = (skillKey: string) => {
      const currentData = character.skills[skillKey];
      const initialValue = currentData?.customName || (normalizedOriginSkills.includes(skillKey) && skillKey === 'Profissão' ? originName : '');
      
      const newName = prompt(`Nome da ${skillKey}:`, initialValue);
      
      if (newName !== null) {
          if (!character.skills[skillKey]) {
              character.skills[skillKey] = { level: 'destreinado', isTrained: false, miscBonus: 0 };
          }
          character.skills[skillKey].customName = newName;
          setForceUpdate(prev => prev + 1);
      }
  };

  // Efeito Principal: Aplica as perícias na ficha
  useEffect(() => {
      if (!selectedClass) return;

      SKILL_LIST.forEach(s => {
          if (!normalizedOriginSkills.includes(s)) {
              if (character.skills[s]) {
                  character.skills[s].isTrained = false;
                  character.skills[s].level = 'destreinado';
              }
          } else {
               if (!character.skills[s]) character.skills[s] = { level: 'treinado', isTrained: true, miscBonus: 0 };
               else { 
                   character.skills[s].isTrained = true; 
                   character.skills[s].level = 'treinado';
                   if (s === 'Profissão' && !character.skills[s].customName) {
                       character.skills[s].customName = originName;
                   }
               }
          }
      });

      if (selectedClass === 'ocultista') {
          ['Ocultismo', 'Vontade'].forEach(s => {
               if (!character.skills[s]) character.skills[s] = { level: 'treinado', isTrained: true, miscBonus: 0 };
               else { character.skills[s].isTrained = true; character.skills[s].level = 'treinado'; }
          });
      }

      if (selectedClass === 'combatente') {
          [combatenteFightChoice, combatenteResistChoice].forEach(s => {
              if (s) {
                if (!character.skills[s]) character.skills[s] = { level: 'treinado', isTrained: true, miscBonus: 0 };
                else { character.skills[s].isTrained = true; character.skills[s].level = 'treinado'; }
              }
          });
      }

      selectedSkills.forEach(s => {
          if (!character.skills[s]) character.skills[s] = { level: 'treinado', isTrained: true, miscBonus: 0 };
          else { character.skills[s].isTrained = true; character.skills[s].level = 'treinado'; }
      });

  }, [selectedClass, selectedSkills, combatenteFightChoice, combatenteResistChoice, originName]);

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full gap-6 animate-in fade-in slide-in-from-right-8 duration-500">
      
      <div className="text-center mb-4">
        <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold text-eden-100">Escolha sua Classe</h2>
        <p className="text-eden-100/50">Define seus PV, PE, Sanidade e Perícias Iniciais.</p>
      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 gap-4">
        <button
          onClick={() => handleClassSelect('combatente')}
          className={`p-6 rounded-2xl border-2 flex flex-col md:flex-row items-start md:items-center gap-6 transition-all text-left group ${selectedClass === 'combatente' ? 'bg-red-600/10 border-red-500' : 'bg-eden-800 border-eden-700 hover:border-eden-500'}`}
        >
          <div className={`p-4 rounded-full bg-eden-900 shrink-0 ${selectedClass === 'combatente' ? 'text-red-500' : 'text-eden-100/50 group-hover:text-white'}`}>
              <Sword size={32} />
          </div>
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-xl font-bold text-white mb-1">Combatente</h3>
            <p className="text-xs text-eden-100/60 mb-2">A linha de frente. Mestre em armas e proteção.</p>
            <div className="text-[10px] text-eden-100/40 space-y-1 font-mono">
                <p>PV: 20 (+4/NEX) | PE: 2 (+2/NEX) | SAN: 12 (+3/NEX)</p>
                <p>Proficiências: Armas Simples e Táticas, Proteções Leves.</p>
                <p>Habilidade Inicial: <strong className="text-red-400">Ataque Especial</strong>.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </button>

        <button
          onClick={() => handleClassSelect('especialista')}
          className={`p-6 rounded-2xl border-2 flex flex-col md:flex-row items-start md:items-center gap-6 transition-all text-left group ${selectedClass === 'especialista' ? 'bg-emerald-600/10 border-emerald-500' : 'bg-eden-800 border-eden-700 hover:border-eden-500'}`}
        >
          <div className="p-4 rounded-full bg-eden-900 text-emerald-500"><Book size={32} /></div>
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-xl font-bold text-white mb-1">Especialista</h3>
            <p className="text-xs text-eden-100/60 mb-2">O mestre das perícias. Técnico, ágil e versátil.</p>
            <div className="text-[10px] text-eden-100/40 space-y-1 font-mono">
                <p>PV: 16 (+3/NEX) | PE: 3 (+3/NEX) | SAN: 16 (+4/NEX)</p>
                <p>Proficiências: Armas Simples, Proteções Leves.</p>
                <p>Habilidade Inicial: <strong className="text-emerald-400">Perito</strong>.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </button>

        <button
          onClick={() => handleClassSelect('ocultista')}
          className={`p-6 rounded-2xl border-2 flex flex-col md:flex-row items-start md:items-center gap-6 transition-all text-left group ${selectedClass === 'ocultista' ? 'bg-violet-600/10 border-violet-500' : 'bg-eden-800 border-eden-700 hover:border-eden-500'}`}
        >
          <div className="p-4 rounded-full bg-eden-900 text-violet-500"><Eye size={32} /></div>
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-xl font-bold text-white mb-1">Ocultista</h3>
            <p className="text-xs text-eden-100/60 mb-2">Estudioso do paranormal. Conjura rituais e controla elementos.</p>
            <div className="text-[10px] text-eden-100/40 space-y-1 font-mono">
                <p>PV: 12 (+2/NEX) | PE: 4 (+4/NEX) | SAN: 20 (+5/NEX)</p>
                <p>Proficiências: Armas Simples.</p>
                <p>Habilidade Inicial: <strong className="text-violet-400">Escolhido pelo Outro Lado</strong>.</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        </button>
      </div>

      {selectedClass && (
        <div className="flex-1 bg-eden-800/50 border border-eden-700 rounded-xl p-6 flex flex-col gap-4 overflow-hidden">
            <div className="flex justify-between items-center border-b border-eden-700 pb-2">
                <h3 className="font-bold text-eden-100">Perícias Treinadas</h3>
                <span className={`text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded font-mono ${selectedSkills.length === freeSlots ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-400' : 'bg-eden-900 text-eden-100/50'}`}>
                    Livres: {selectedSkills.length} / {freeSlots}
                </span>
            </div>

            {selectedClass === 'combatente' && (needsFightChoice || needsResistChoice) && (
                <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4 mb-2">
                    {needsFightChoice && (
                        <div className="bg-eden-900/50 p-3 rounded border border-red-500/30">
                            <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-red-400 block mb-2 uppercase">Estilo de Combate</span>
                            <div className="flex gap-2">
                                <button onClick={() => setCombatenteFightChoice('Luta')} className={`flex-1 py-2 text-xs rounded border transition-colors ${combatenteFightChoice === 'Luta' ? 'bg-red-500 text-white border-red-500' : 'border-eden-600 text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-800'}`}>Luta</button>
                                <button onClick={() => setCombatenteFightChoice('Pontaria')} className={`flex-1 py-2 text-xs rounded border transition-colors ${combatenteFightChoice === 'Pontaria' ? 'bg-red-500 text-white border-red-500' : 'border-eden-600 text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-800'}`}>Pontaria</button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    )}
                    {needsResistChoice && (
                        <div className="bg-eden-900/50 p-3 rounded border border-red-500/30">
                            <span className="text-[10px] font-bold text-red-400 block mb-2 uppercase">Resistência</span>
                            <div className="flex gap-2">
                                <button onClick={() => setCombatenteResistChoice('Fortitude')} className={`flex-1 py-2 text-xs rounded border transition-colors ${combatenteResistChoice === 'Fortitude' ? 'bg-red-500 text-white border-red-500' : 'border-eden-600 text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-800'}`}>Fortitude</button>
                                <button onClick={() => setCombatenteResistChoice('Reflexos')} className={`flex-1 py-2 text-xs rounded border transition-colors ${combatenteResistChoice === 'Reflexos' ? 'bg-red-500 text-white border-red-500' : 'border-eden-600 text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-800'}`}>Reflexos</button>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    )}
                </div>
            )}

            <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-2 overflow-y-auto custom-scrollbar pr-2">
                {SKILL_LIST.map(skill => {
                    const isOrigin = normalizedOriginSkills.includes(skill);
                    const isAuto = selectedClass === 'ocultista' && (skill === 'Ocultismo' || skill === 'Vontade');
                    const isSelected = selectedSkills.includes(skill);
                    const isCombatChoice = (combatenteFightChoice === skill) || (combatenteResistChoice === skill);
                    const isProfession = skill.startsWith('Profissão');

                    // Recupera nome customizado (para exibir se já tiver sido editado)
                    const currentName = character.skills[skill]?.customName;

                    let stateClass = 'border-eden-700 text-eden-100/40 hover:border-eden-500 hover:bg-eden-700/30'; 
                    let icon = null;

                    if (isOrigin) {
                        stateClass = 'bg-amber-500/10 border-amber-500/50 text-amber-200 cursor-default';
                        icon = <span className="text-[8px] uppercase font-bold opacity-70">Origem</span>;
                    } else if (isAuto) {
                        stateClass = 'bg-violet-500/10 border-violet-500/50 text-violet-200 cursor-default';
                        icon = <span className="text-[8px] uppercase font-bold opacity-70">Classe</span>;
                    } else if (isCombatChoice) {
                        stateClass = 'bg-red-500/10 border-red-500/50 text-red-200 cursor-default';
                        icon = <Check size={12}/>;
                    } else if (isSelected) {
                        stateClass = 'bg-eden-100 text-eden-900 border-eden-100 font-bold shadow-md';
                        icon = <Check size={12}/>;
                    }

                    const isTrained = isOrigin || isAuto || isCombatChoice || isSelected;

                    return (
                        <div key={skill} className="relative group">
                            <button
                                onClick={() => toggleSkill(skill)}
                                disabled={isOrigin || isAuto || isCombatChoice}
                                className={`w-full text-left px-3 py-2.5 rounded-lg text-xs flex justify-between items-center border transition-all ${stateClass}`}
                            >
                                <span className="truncate pr-4">
                                    {skill} 
                                    {currentName && <span className="block text-[9px] italic opacity-70">({currentName})</span>}
                                </span>
                                {icon}
                            </button>
                            
                            {/* Botão de Lápis para Profissões Treinadas */}
                            {isProfession && isTrained && (
                                <button 
                                    onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); renameSkill(skill); }}
                                    className="absolute right-1 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 p-1 rounded-full bg-eden-900/80 text-eden-100 hover:text-energia border border-eden-600 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-all z-10"
                                    title="Definir Profissão"
                                >
                                    <Pencil size={10} />
                                </button>
                            )}
                        </div>
                    )
                })}
            </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {selectedClass && selectedSkills.length < freeSlots && (
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-yellow-400 text-xs justify-center animate-pulse">
              <AlertTriangle size={14} />
              Escolha mais {freeSlots - selectedSkills.length} perícias para continuar.
          </div>
      )}

    </div>
  );
}

      </div>

      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-8 flex-1">
        
        {/* COLUNA ESQUERDA: Foto e Identidade */}
        <div className="space-y-6">
          
          {/* Card de Retrato */}

              {/* A Foto em Si */}

                {info.portraitUrl ? (
                  <img 
                    src={info.portraitUrl} 
                    alt={info.name} 
                    className="w-full h-full object-cover"
                    onError={(e) => {
                      // Fallback se a imagem quebrar
                      (e.target as HTMLImageElement).src = ''; 
                      updateInfo('portraitUrl', ''); // Limpa no estado
                    }}
                  />
                ) : (
                  <User size={64} className="text-eden-700" />
                )}

                <ImageIcon size={12} /> URL da Imagem
              </label>
              <input
                type="text"
                value={info.portraitUrl}
                onChange={(e) => updateInfo('portraitUrl', e.target.value)}
                placeholder="https://..."
                className="w-full bg-eden-900/50 border border-eden-700 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm text-eden-100 focus:border-energia focus:ring-1 focus:ring-energia outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-eden-100/20"
              />

              </p>
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* Dica de Roleplay */}
          <div className="bg-eden-900/30 border border-eden-700/30 rounded-xl p-4 flex gap-3 items-start">
            <Sparkles className="w-5 h-5 text-conhecimento shrink-0 mt-0.5" />
            <div className="space-y-1">
              <h4 className="text-sm font-bold text-conhecimento">Dica de Interpretação</h4>
              <p className="text-xs text-eden-100/60 leading-relaxed">
                Pense em defeitos tanto quanto qualidades. Um agente perfeito é chato; um agente com medos e vícios é memorável.
              </p>
            </div>

        </div>

        {/* COLUNA DIREITA: Textos Longos */}

              <User className="w-4 h-4 text-energia" /> Aparência Física
            </label>
            <textarea
              value={info.appearance}
              onChange={(e) => updateInfo('appearance', e.target.value)}
              className="w-full h-24 bg-eden-800 border border-eden-700 rounded-xl p-4 text-eden-100 focus:border-energia focus:ring-1 focus:ring-energia outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-eden-100/20 resize-none"

          <div className="space-y-2">
            <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm font-medium text-eden-100/70">
              <Sparkles className="w-4 h-4 text-conhecimento" /> Personalidade
            </label>
            <textarea
              value={info.personality}
              onChange={(e) => updateInfo('personality', e.target.value)}
              className="w-full h-24 bg-eden-800 border border-eden-700 rounded-xl p-4 text-eden-100 focus:border-conhecimento focus:ring-1 focus:ring-conhecimento outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-eden-100/20 resize-none"
              placeholder="Como seu personagem age? Ele é calmo, explosivo, metódico? O que ele teme?"

          {/* Histórico */}

              <Scroll className="w-4 h-4 text-sangue" /> Histórico (Backstory)
            </label>
            <textarea
              value={info.history}
              onChange={(e) => updateInfo('history', e.target.value)}
              className="w-full flex-1 min-h-[150px] bg-eden-800 border border-eden-700 rounded-xl p-4 text-eden-100 focus:border-sangue focus:ring-1 focus:ring-sangue outline-none transition-all placeholder:text-eden-100/20 resize-none"

========================================
FILE: Step6Inventory.tsx
PATH: D:\Programs\eden-arquivos\eden-arquivos\src\components\wizard\Step6Inventory.tsx
