FILE: CreateSheet.tsx
PATH: D:\Programs\eden-arquivos\eden-arquivos\src\pages\CreateSheet.tsx
========================================
import { useState } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { CharacterProvider, useCharacter } from '../context/CharacterContext';
import { ChevronRight, ChevronLeft, Save, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import { saveCharacter } from '../services/characterService';

// Importação dos Passos
import Step1Concept from '../components/wizard/Step1Concept';
import Step2Attributes from '../components/wizard/Step2Attributes';
import Step3Origins from '../components/wizard/Step3Origins';
import Step4Classes from '../components/wizard/Step4Classes';
import Step5Details from '../components/wizard/Step5Details';
import Step6Inventory from '../components/wizard/Step6Inventory';
import Step7Rituals from '../components/wizard/Step7Rituals';
import Step8Team from '../components/wizard/Step8Team';

// Componente Interno para acessar o Contexto
function WizardContent() {
  const [step, setStep] = useState(1);
  const [isSaving, setIsSaving] = useState(false);
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const { character } = useCharacter();

  const handleNext = async () => {
    if (step < 8) {
      setStep(s => s + 1);
    } else {
      // FINALIZAR E SALVAR
      setIsSaving(true);
      try {
        const id = await saveCharacter(character);
        // Redirecionamento Automático para a Ficha
        navigate(`/ficha/${id}`); 
      } catch (error) {
        console.error(error); // Log para debug
        alert("Erro ao salvar. Verifique o console.");
        setIsSaving(false);
      }
    }
  };

  const renderStep = () => {
    switch(step) {
      case 1: return <Step1Concept />;
      case 2: return <Step2Attributes />;
      case 3: return <Step3Origins />;
      case 4: return <Step4Classes />;
      case 5: return <Step5Details />;
      case 6: return <Step6Inventory />;
      case 7: return <Step7Rituals />;
      case 8: return <Step8Team />;
      default: return null;
    }
  };

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-eden-900 text-eden-100 flex flex-col">
      {/* Barra de Progresso */}
      <div className="w-full bg-eden-800 h-2">
        <div 
          className="bg-gradient-to-r from-energia to-conhecimento h-full transition-all duration-500"
          style={{ width: `${(step / 8) * 100}%` }}
        />
      </div>

      <main className="flex-1 max-w-6xl w-full mx-auto p-4 md:p-6 flex flex-col h-[calc(100vh-8px)]">
        {/* Header */}
        <header className="flex justify-between items-center mb-4 border-b border-eden-700 pb-4 shrink-0">
          <button onClick={() => navigate('/')} className="text-sm text-eden-100/50 hover:text-eden-100 transition-colors">
            &larr; Cancelar
          </button>
          <span className="text-sm font-mono text-eden-100/30">PROTOCOLO {step}/8</span>
        </header>

        {/* Área de Conteúdo (Com scroll interno se necessário, mas os passos já tratam isso) */}
        <div className="flex-1 bg-eden-800/30 border border-eden-700 rounded-2xl p-4 md:p-6 shadow-2xl mb-4 overflow-hidden relative">
          {renderStep()}
        </div>

        {/* Navegação */}
        <div className="flex justify-between items-center shrink-0">
          <button
            onClick={() => step > 1 ? setStep(s => s - 1) : null}
            disabled={step === 1 || isSaving}
            className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-semibold transition-all ${
              step === 1 ? 'opacity-0 pointer-events-none' : 'bg-eden-700 hover:bg-eden-600 text-eden-100'
            }`}
          >
            <ChevronLeft className="w-5 h-5" /> Anterior
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={handleNext}
            disabled={isSaving}
            className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-8 py-3 rounded-lg font-bold transition-all shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(255,255,255,0.1)] ${
               step === 8 
               ? 'bg-energia text-eden-900 hover:bg-yellow-400' 
               : 'bg-eden-100 text-eden-900 hover:bg-white hover:scale-105'
            }`}
          >
            {isSaving ? (
              <><Loader2 className="w-5 h-5 animate-spin" /> Salvando...</>
            ) : step === 8 ? (
              <><Save className="w-5 h-5" /> Finalizar Protocolo</>
            ) : (
              <>Próximo <ChevronRight className="w-5 h-5" /></>
            )}
          </button>
        </div>
      </main>
    </div>
  );
}

// Wrapper Principal
export default function CreateSheet() {
  return (
    <CharacterProvider>
      <WizardContent />
    </CharacterProvider>
  );
}

FILE: Home.tsx
PATH: D:\Programs\eden-arquivos\eden-arquivos\src\pages\Home.tsx
========================================
import { useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { collection, getDocs, query, orderBy } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { Sword, Book, Plus, Scroll, Ghost, Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';
import type { CharacterSheet } from '../types/characterSchema';

export default function Home() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [characters, setCharacters] = useState<CharacterSheet[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    async function fetchCharacters() {
      try {
        const q = query(collection(db, "characters"), orderBy("createdAt", "desc"));
        const querySnapshot = await getDocs(q);
        
        const chars: CharacterSheet[] = [];
        querySnapshot.forEach((doc) => {
          // CORREÇÃO CRÍTICA: ...doc.data() vem PRIMEIRO, doc.id vem DEPOIS
          // Isso garante que o ID real do Firestore sobrescreva qualquer ID vazio salvo por engano
          chars.push({ ...doc.data(), id: doc.id } as CharacterSheet);
        });
        
        setCharacters(chars);
      } catch (error) {
        console.error("Erro ao buscar fichas:", error);
      } finally {
        setLoading(false);
      }
    }

    fetchCharacters();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen flex flex-col bg-eden-900 text-eden-100">
      
      {/* Hero Section */}
      <div className="bg-eden-800 border-b border-eden-700 py-12 px-6 text-center relative overflow-hidden">
        <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-[url('https://www.transparenttextures.com/patterns/cubes.png')] opacity-5 pointer-events-none"></div>
        <h1 className="text-6xl font-black tracking-tighter text-transparent bg-clip-text bg-gradient-to-br from-eden-100 to-eden-500 mb-2 relative z-10">
          EDEN
        </h1>
        <p className="text-xl text-eden-100/40 font-mono tracking-[0.5em] uppercase relative z-10">
          Arquivos Paranormais
        </p>
      </div>

      <main className="flex-1 max-w-6xl w-full mx-auto p-8">
        
        {/* Ações */}
        <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-3 gap-6 mb-12">
            <button 
                onClick={() => navigate('/criar')}
                className="group relative overflow-hidden p-8 bg-eden-800 border border-eden-600 rounded-2xl hover:border-energia transition-all hover:shadow-[0_0_30px_-10px_rgba(124,58,237,0.3)] text-left"
            >
                <div className="absolute top-0 right-0 p-4 opacity-10 group-hover:opacity-20 transition-opacity">
                    <Plus size={100} />
                </div>
                <div className="p-3 bg-eden-900/80 rounded-lg w-fit mb-4 group-hover:bg-energia group-hover:text-eden-900 transition-colors">
                    <Sword size={32} />
                </div>
                <h3 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-1">Nova Missão</h3>
                <p className="text-eden-100/50 text-sm">Iniciar protocolo de criação de agente.</p>
            </button>

            <button disabled className="group relative overflow-hidden p-8 bg-eden-800/50 border border-eden-700 rounded-2xl text-left opacity-60 cursor-not-allowed">
                <div className="p-3 bg-eden-900/80 rounded-lg w-fit mb-4">
                    <Book size={32} />
                </div>
                <h3 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-1">Compêndio</h3>
                <p className="text-eden-100/50 text-sm">Acesso ao banco de dados (Em breve).</p>
            </button>
             
            <div className="p-8 bg-eden-900 border border-eden-700 rounded-2xl flex flex-col justify-center items-center text-center">
                <span className="text-4xl font-black text-eden-100">{characters.length}</span>
                <span className="text-xs uppercase tracking-widest text-eden-100/40">Agentes Ativos</span>
            </div>
        </div>

        {/* Lista */}
        <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-eden-100 mb-6 flex items-center gap-3 border-b border-eden-700 pb-4">
            <Scroll className="text-conhecimento" /> Arquivos Recentes
        </h2>

        {loading ? (
            <div className="flex justify-center py-20 text-eden-100/30">
                <Loader2 size={48} className="animate-spin" />
            </div>
        ) : characters.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="text-center py-20 bg-eden-800/30 rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-eden-700">
                <Ghost size={64} className="mx-auto mb-4 text-eden-100/20" />
                <p className="text-lg text-eden-100/50">Nenhum agente encontrado nos registros.</p>
            </div>
        ) : (
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
                {characters.map(char => (
                    <button 
                        key={char.id}
                        onClick={() => navigate(`/ficha/${char.id}`)}
                        className="flex items-center gap-4 p-4 bg-eden-800 border border-eden-700 rounded-xl hover:border-eden-500 hover:bg-eden-700 transition-all group text-left"
                    >
                        <div className="w-16 h-16 rounded-full bg-eden-900 overflow-hidden border-2 border-eden-600 group-hover:border-eden-400 shrink-0">
                            {char.info.portraitUrl ? (
                                <img src={char.info.portraitUrl} alt={char.info.name} className="w-full h-full object-cover" />
                            ) : (
                                <div className="w-full h-full flex items-center justify-center text-eden-100/20"><Ghost /></div>
                            )}
                        </div>
                        
                        <div className="min-w-0">
                            <h4 className="font-bold text-lg text-eden-100 truncate group-hover:text-white">{char.info.name || 'Desconhecido'}</h4>
                            <div className="flex gap-2 text-xs text-eden-100/50 font-mono uppercase mt-1">
                                <span>{char.progression.nex}%</span>
                                <span>•</span>
                                <span>{char.progression.class}</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </button>
                ))}
            </div>
        )}

      </main>
    </div>
  );
}

import { useEffect, useState, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useParams, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { doc, getDoc, updateDoc } from 'firebase/firestore';
import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import type { CharacterSheet, DamageType } from '../types/characterSchema';
import { 
  Shield, Brain, Zap, Eye, BicepsFlexed, Ghost, ArrowLeft, Edit2, Save, 
  Footprints, Swords, Backpack, Dice5, Plus, X, BookOpen, Play, User, Users, PenTool 
} from 'lucide-react';

// Componentes
import SheetStatus from '../components/sheet/SheetStatus';
import ConditionsCard from '../components/sheet/ConditionsCard';
import SheetSkills from '../components/sheet/SheetSkills';
import SheetInventory from '../components/sheet/SheetInventory';
import SheetRituals from '../components/sheet/SheetRituals';
import SheetCombat from '../components/sheet/SheetCombat';
import type { CombatState } from '../components/sheet/SheetCombat';
import SheetDescription from '../components/sheet/SheetDescription';
import SheetTeam from '../components/sheet/SheetTeam';
import SheetAbilities from '../components/sheet/SheetAbilities';
import SheetNotes from '../components/sheet/SheetNotes';
import LevelUpModal from '../components/leveling/LevelUpModal';

// Dados
import { DAMAGE_TYPES_INFO } from '../data/referenceData';
import { TRAILS } from '../data/trails'; // Importante para desfazer trilhas

const ATTR_CONFIG = {
  agi: { label: 'AGI', icon: Zap, color: 'text-yellow-400' },
  for: { label: 'FOR', icon: BicepsFlexed, color: 'text-red-500' },
  int: { label: 'INT', icon: Brain, color: 'text-blue-400' },
  pre: { label: 'PRE', icon: Eye, color: 'text-purple-400' },
  vig: { label: 'VIG', icon: Shield, color: 'text-green-500' },
};

const ATTRIBUTE_ORDER: (keyof typeof ATTR_CONFIG)[] = ['agi', 'for', 'int', 'pre', 'vig'];

type DeepPartial<T> = { [P in keyof T]?: T[P] extends object ? DeepPartial<T[P]> : T[P]; };

export default function Sheet() {
  const { id } = useParams();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [character, setCharacter] = useState<CharacterSheet | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<'skills' | 'inventory' | 'combat' | 'rituals' | 'description' | 'team' | 'abilities' | 'notes'>('skills');
  const [isEditingHeader, setIsEditingHeader] = useState(false);
  const [tempName, setTempName] = useState('');
  const [tempPlayer, setTempPlayer] = useState('');

  const [showResistModal, setShowResistModal] = useState(false);
  const [selectedDmgType, setSelectedDmgType] = useState<string>(DAMAGE_TYPES_INFO[0].id);
  const [resistValue, setResistValue] = useState<string>('5');
  const [isImmune, setIsImmune] = useState(false);

  const [showLevelUp, setShowLevelUp] = useState(false);
  const [targetLevel, setTargetLevel] = useState(0);

  const [combatState, setCombatState] = useState<CombatState>({
      expandedWeapon: null,
      attackMode: {},
      unbridledMode: {},
      rollResult: null,
      damageMode: 'roll',
      attachedAmmo: {},
      ammoCounters: {},
      ammoLeftovers: {},
      ammoSceneTracker: {}
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    if (!id) { navigate('/'); return; }
    async function fetchSheet() {
      try {
        const docRef = doc(db, "characters", id!);
        const docSnap = await getDoc(docRef);
        if (docSnap.exists()) {
          const data = docSnap.data() as CharacterSheet;
          if (!data.status.sustainedIds) data.status.sustainedIds = [];
          if (data.progression.nex > 99) data.progression.nex = 99;
          
          setCharacter(data);
          setTempName(data.info.name);
          setTempPlayer(data.info.player);
        } else {
          alert("Ficha não encontrada!");
          navigate('/');
        }
      } catch (error) { console.error("Erro:", error); } finally { setLoading(false); }
    }
    fetchSheet();
  }, [id, navigate]);

  const handleUpdate = useCallback(async (updates: DeepPartial<CharacterSheet>) => {
    if (!character || !id) return;
    const updatedChar = { ...character, ...updates } as CharacterSheet;
    setCharacter(updatedChar);
    try { await updateDoc(doc(db, "characters", id), updates as any); } catch (e) { console.error(e); }
  }, [character, id]);

  const saveHeader = () => {
    handleUpdate({ info: { ...character!.info, name: tempName, player: tempPlayer } });
    setIsEditingHeader(false);
  };

  const handleNextTurn = () => {
      if (!character) return;
      const sustainedCount = character.status.sustainedIds?.length || 0;
      const peLoss = sustainedCount; 
      const newPE = Math.max(0, character.status.pe.current - peLoss);
      const updatedConditions = character.status.conditions.map(c => {
        if (c.durationType === 'turnos' && c.durationValue !== undefined) {
          return { ...c, durationValue: c.durationValue - 1 };
        }
        return c;
      }).filter(c => c.durationType !== 'turnos' || (c.durationValue !== undefined && c.durationValue > 0));
      handleUpdate({
          status: {
              ...character.status,
              pe: { ...character.status.pe, current: newPE },
              conditions: updatedConditions
          }
      });
      let msg = "Novo turno iniciado.";
      if (sustainedCount > 0) msg += `\n-${sustainedCount} PE por sustentação (${sustainedCount} ativos).`;
      if (character.status.conditions.length > 0) msg += `\nLembre-se de calcular efeitos das condições!`;
      alert(msg);
  };
  
  // --- LÓGICA DE REDUÇÃO DE NEX (CORRIGIDA) ---
  const handleUndoLevel = () => {
    if(!character) return;
    const currentNex = character.progression.nex;
    const prevNex = Math.max(5, currentNex - 5);
    
    if (currentNex === 5) return;

    if(!confirm(`ATENÇÃO: Você está prestes a rebaixar o NEX para ${prevNex}%.
    O sistema irá reverter:
    - PV/PE/SAN máximos.
    - Poderes de Classe recentes.
    - Trilhas (se NEX 10).
    - Atributos (se aumentados neste nível).
    
    Perícias devem ser ajustadas manualmente.`)) {
        return;
    }

    const updates: any = { 
        progression: { ...character.progression, nex: prevNex },
        status: { ...character.status },
        classPowers: { ...character.classPowers },
        attributes: { ...character.attributes }
    };

    // 1. REVERTER PV/PE/SAN
    let pvLoss = 2 + character.attributes.vig;
    let peLoss = 2 + character.attributes.pre;
    let sanLoss = 3;

    if (character.progression.class === 'combatente') { pvLoss = 4 + character.attributes.vig; peLoss = 2 + character.attributes.pre; sanLoss = 3; }
    if (character.progression.class === 'especialista') { pvLoss = 3 + character.attributes.vig; peLoss = 3 + character.attributes.pre; sanLoss = 4; }
    if (character.progression.class === 'ocultista') { pvLoss = 2 + character.attributes.vig; peLoss = 4 + character.attributes.pre; sanLoss = 5; }

    updates.status.pv.max = Math.max(1, character.status.pv.max - pvLoss);
    updates.status.pv.current = Math.max(1, character.status.pv.current - pvLoss);
    updates.status.pe.max = Math.max(1, character.status.pe.max - peLoss);
    updates.status.pe.current = Math.max(0, character.status.pe.current - peLoss);
    updates.status.san.max = Math.max(1, character.status.san.max - sanLoss);
    updates.status.san.current = Math.max(0, character.status.san.current - sanLoss);

    // 2. REVERTER ATRIBUTOS (Usando o histórico salvo)
    const attrHistory = character.progression.attributeIncreases || {};
    const attrIncreasedAtCurrentNex = attrHistory[currentNex]; // Verifica se houve aumento NO NÍVEL ATUAL (o que estamos removendo)

    if (attrIncreasedAtCurrentNex) {
        // Reduz o atributo
        updates.attributes[attrIncreasedAtCurrentNex] -= 1;
        
        // Remove do histórico
        const newHistory = { ...attrHistory };
        delete newHistory[currentNex];
        updates.progression.attributeIncreases = newHistory;
    }

    // 3. REVERTER PODERES DE CLASSE
    if (currentNex % 15 === 0 && updates.classPowers.selectedIds.length > 0) {
        updates.classPowers.selectedIds.pop();
    }

    // 4. REVERTER TRILHA
    if (currentNex === 10) {
        updates.progression.trail = '';
        const trailData = TRAILS.find(t => t.id === character.progression.trail);
        if (trailData) {
            const p10 = trailData.abilities.find(a => a.nex === 10);
            if (p10) updates.classPowers.selectedIds = updates.classPowers.selectedIds.filter((id: string) => id !== p10.name);
        }
    }

    // 5. REVERTER PODER DE TRILHA
    if ([40, 65, 99].includes(currentNex)) {
         const trailData = TRAILS.find(t => t.id === character.progression.trail);
         if (trailData) {
             const ability = trailData.abilities.find(a => a.nex === currentNex);
             if (ability) updates.classPowers.selectedIds = updates.classPowers.selectedIds.filter((id: string) => id !== ability.name);
         }
    }
    
    // 6. REVERTER UPGRADE DE CLASSE
    if (currentNex === 25) {
        updates.classPowers.coreLevel = Math.max(0, (character.classPowers.coreLevel || 0) - 1);
    }

    handleUpdate(updates);
  };

  const calculateStats = () => {
    if (!character) return { def: 0, esquiva: 0, move: 0, movimentacoes: 0, peLimit: 0 };
    let def = 10 + character.attributes.agi + character.status.defense.passiveMod + character.status.defense.tempMod;
    let move = character.status.displacement.baseMetres + character.status.displacement.tempMod;
    let peLimit = Math.ceil(character.progression.nex / 5);

    character.status.conditions.forEach(c => {
        if (['Vulnerável', 'Caído', 'Atordoado', 'Desprevenido', 'Cego', 'Agarrado'].includes(c.name)) def -= (c.effects?.[0]?.value || 0) * -1; 
        if (['Lento'].includes(c.name)) move /= 2;
        if (['Imóvel', 'Paralisado'].includes(c.name)) move = 0;
    });

    const movimentacoes = Math.floor(move / 1.5);
    return { def, move, movimentacoes, peLimit };
  };

  const handleAddResistance = () => {
    if (!character) return;
    const type = selectedDmgType as DamageType;
    const value = parseInt(resistValue) || 0;
    const newResistances = { ...character.status.resistances };
    let newImmunities = [...character.status.immunities];
    if (isImmune) {
        if (!newImmunities.includes(type)) newImmunities.push(type);
        delete newResistances[type];
    } else {
        newResistances[type] = value;
        newImmunities = newImmunities.filter(i => i !== type);
    }
    handleUpdate({ status: { ...character.status, resistances: newResistances, immunities: newImmunities } });
    setShowResistModal(false);
  };

  const removeResistance = (type: DamageType, isImmunity: boolean) => {
      if (!character) return;
      if (isImmunity) {
          handleUpdate({ status: { ...character.status, immunities: character.status.immunities.filter(i => i !== type) } });
      } else {
          const newRes = { ...character.status.resistances };
          delete newRes[type];
          handleUpdate({ status: { ...character.status, resistances: newRes } });
      }
  };

  if (loading || !character) return <div className="min-h-screen bg-eden-900 flex items-center justify-center text-eden-100">Carregando...</div>;

  const stats = calculateStats();
  const selectedDmgData = DAMAGE_TYPES_INFO.find(d => d.id === selectedDmgType);
  const INPUT_STYLE = "w-full bg-eden-950 text-eden-100 border border-eden-700 rounded p-2 text-sm outline-none focus:border-energia placeholder-eden-100/30";

  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-eden-900 text-eden-100 pb-20 font-sans selection:bg-energia selection:text-eden-900">
      
      {/* HEADER */}
      <header className="bg-eden-800/90 backdrop-blur-md border-b border-eden-700 p-4 sticky top-0 z-50 shadow-lg">
        <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto w-full">
            
            {/* LINHA 1: DISTRIBUIÇÃO IGUAL (JUSTIFY-BETWEEN) */}
            <div className="flex flex-col xl:flex-row justify-between items-center gap-6 w-full">
                
                {/* 1. ESQUERDA: IDENTIDADE */}
                <div className="flex items-center gap-5 shrink-0 self-start xl:self-center">
                    <button onClick={() => navigate('/')} className="p-2 hover:bg-eden-700 rounded-full transition-colors shrink-0 text-eden-100/50 hover:text-white"><ArrowLeft size={28} /></button>
                    
                    <div className="relative group cursor-pointer shrink-0">
                        <div className="w-20 h-20 rounded-full overflow-hidden border-2 border-eden-500 bg-eden-900 shadow-lg">
                            {character.info.portraitUrl ? <img src={character.info.portraitUrl} className="w-full h-full object-cover" /> : <div className="flex items-center justify-center h-full"><Ghost size={32} className="text-eden-700"/></div>}
                        </div>
                    </div>

                    <div className="min-w-[150px]">
                        {isEditingHeader ? (
                            <div className="flex flex-col gap-2 animate-in fade-in">
                                <input value={tempName} onChange={e => setTempName(e.target.value)} className="bg-eden-950 border border-eden-600 rounded px-3 py-1 text-xl font-bold w-full text-eden-100 outline-none focus:border-energia" placeholder="Nome do Personagem" style={{ colorScheme: 'dark' }} />
                                <div className="flex gap-2">
                                    <input value={tempPlayer} onChange={e => setTempPlayer(e.target.value)} className="bg-eden-950 border border-eden-600 rounded px-2 py-1 text-sm w-full text-eden-100 outline-none focus:border-energia" placeholder="Nome do Jogador" style={{ colorScheme: 'dark' }} />
                                    <button onClick={saveHeader} className="bg-energia text-eden-900 text-xs font-bold rounded px-3 py-1 flex items-center gap-1 hover:bg-yellow-400"><Save size={14}/> Salvar</button>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        ) : (
                            <div className="group relative">
                                <h1 className="text-3xl lg:text-4xl font-black uppercase tracking-wide leading-none flex items-center gap-2 truncate text-white">
                                    {character.info.name || "Sem Nome"}
                                    <button onClick={() => setIsEditingHeader(true)} className="opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 transition-opacity p-1 hover:bg-eden-700 rounded text-eden-100/50"><Edit2 size={18}/></button>
                                </h1>
                                <div className="text-sm text-eden-100/60 font-mono flex flex-wrap gap-3 items-center mt-1 font-bold">
                                    <span>{character.info.player || "Jogador"}</span>
                                    <span className="w-1.5 h-1.5 rounded-full bg-eden-600"/>
                                    <span className="text-energia font-black uppercase tracking-wider">{character.progression.class}</span>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        )}
                    </div>
                </div>

                {/* 2. CENTRO: ATRIBUTOS */}
                <div className="flex items-center justify-center bg-eden-950/60 px-8 py-3 rounded-2xl border border-eden-700/50 shadow-inner backdrop-blur-sm shrink-0 gap-6 xl:gap-10">
                    {ATTRIBUTE_ORDER.map((key) => {
                        const { color, label, icon: Icon } = ATTR_CONFIG[key];
                        return (
                            <div key={key} className="flex flex-col items-center gap-1 min-w-[32px]">
                                <span className={`text-[10px] font-black tracking-widest ${color} flex items-center gap-1 uppercase opacity-80`}><Icon size={12} /> {label}</span>
                                <div className="text-4xl font-black text-eden-100 leading-none drop-shadow-lg">{character.attributes[key]}</div>
                            </div>
                        );
                    })}
                </div>

                {/* 3. DIREITA: BOTÕES */}
                <div className="flex gap-3 shrink-0 self-end xl:self-center">
                     <button 
                          onClick={handleNextTurn}
                          className="h-16 px-6 bg-eden-800 hover:bg-eden-700 text-eden-100 border-2 border-eden-600 rounded-2xl font-bold text-sm flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1 transition-all hover:scale-105 shadow-lg active:scale-95"
                          title="Passar Turno"
                      >
                          <Play size={20} fill="currentColor" /> PRÓXIMO TURNO
                      </button>
                      
                      {character.progression.nex < 99 && (
                          <button 
                              onClick={() => { setTargetLevel(character.progression.nex + 5); setShowLevelUp(true); }}
                              className="h-16 px-6 bg-energia hover:bg-yellow-400 text-eden-900 rounded-2xl font-black text-sm flex flex-col items-center justify-center gap-1 shadow-[0_0_15px_rgba(234,179,8,0.3)] transition-all hover:scale-105 active:scale-95"
                          >
                              <Plus size={24} strokeWidth={4} /> LEVEL UP
                          </button>
                      )}
                </div>

            </div>

            {/* LINHA 2: STATUS SECUNDÁRIOS */}
            <div className="w-full flex items-center justify-between bg-eden-950/40 border border-eden-700/50 rounded-xl px-8 py-3 mt-2">
                
                {/* NEX (Centralizado) */}
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center relative group cursor-help flex-1">
                     <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-eden-100/40 tracking-wider text-center mb-0.5">Nível de Exposição</span>
                     <div className="text-2xl font-black text-white leading-none text-center relative">
                         {character.progression.nex}%
                         <button onClick={handleUndoLevel} className="absolute -bottom-3 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 opacity-0 group-hover:opacity-100 text-[8px] text-red-500 hover:underline font-bold transition-opacity whitespace-nowrap bg-eden-900 px-1 rounded">DESFAZER</button>
                     </div>
                </div>

                <div className="w-px h-8 bg-eden-700/50"></div>

                {/* PP */}
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center cursor-pointer hover:bg-eden-800/50 rounded px-4 transition-colors flex-1" onClick={() => {
                    const newPP = prompt("Novo valor de Prestígio:", character.progression.prestigePoints.toString());
                    if (newPP && !isNaN(parseInt(newPP))) handleUpdate({ progression: { ...character.progression, prestigePoints: parseInt(newPP) } });
                }}>
                     <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-eden-100/40 tracking-wider text-center mb-0.5">Prestígio</span>
                     <div className="text-2xl font-black text-conhecimento leading-none text-center">{character.progression.prestigePoints}</div>
                </div>

                <div className="w-px h-8 bg-eden-700/50"></div>

                {/* Limite PE */}
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center flex-1">
                     <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-eden-100/40 tracking-wider text-center mb-0.5">Limite PE/Rodada</span>
                     <div className="text-2xl font-black text-yellow-500 leading-none text-center">{stats.peLimit}</div>
                </div>

                <div className="w-px h-8 bg-eden-700/50"></div>

                {/* Campanha */}
                <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center flex-1">
                     <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-eden-100/40 tracking-wider text-center mb-0.5">Campanha</span>
                     <div className="text-sm font-bold text-white leading-none truncate max-w-[250px] text-center py-1">{character.info.campaign || "-"}</div>
                </div>

            </div>

        </div>
      </header>

      <main className="max-w-7xl mx-auto p-4 md:p-6 grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-12 gap-6">
        <div className="lg:col-span-4 space-y-6">
          <div className="bg-eden-800 border border-eden-700 p-4 rounded-xl flex justify-between items-center shadow-sm">
             <div><div className="text-[10px] text-eden-100/50 uppercase tracking-wider font-bold">Trilha</div><div className="font-bold text-energia capitalize text-sm">{character.progression.trail || 'Nenhuma'}</div></div>
             <div><div className="text-[10px] text-eden-100/50 uppercase tracking-wider font-bold text-right">Origem</div><div className="font-bold text-white capitalize text-sm text-right">{character.progression.origin.name}</div></div>
          </div>
          
          <SheetStatus character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} />
          
          <div className="bg-eden-800 border border-eden-700 p-5 rounded-xl shadow-sm space-y-4">
             <div className="flex justify-between items-center pb-4 border-b border-eden-700">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                    <div className="p-2 bg-eden-950 rounded-lg border border-eden-600 text-eden-100 shadow-inner"><Shield size={24}/></div>
                    <div><div className="text-3xl font-black leading-none text-white">{stats.def}</div><div className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-eden-100/40 tracking-widest">Defesa</div></div>
                </div>
                <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-right">
                    <div><div className="text-3xl font-black leading-none text-white">{stats.move}m</div><div className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-eden-100/40 tracking-widest">{stats.movimentacoes} Movimentos</div></div>
                    <div className="p-2 bg-eden-950 rounded-lg border border-eden-600 text-eden-100 shadow-inner"><Footprints size={24}/></div>
                </div>
             </div>
             
             <div className="text-xs text-eden-100/60">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-2">
                    <span className="text-[10px] uppercase font-bold text-eden-100/30 tracking-widest">Resistências & Imunidades</span>
                    <button onClick={() => setShowResistModal(true)} className="p-1 hover:bg-eden-700 rounded text-eden-100/50 hover:text-energia transition-colors" title="Adicionar Resistência"><Plus size={14} /></button>
                </div>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1">
                    {Object.entries(character.status.resistances).map(([k, v]) => v > 0 && (
                        <span key={k} className="group relative px-2 py-1 bg-eden-900 rounded border border-eden-700 capitalize text-xs font-medium text-eden-100 shadow-sm flex items-center gap-1">
                            Resistência à {k} {v}
                            <button onClick={() => removeResistance(k as DamageType, false)} className="hidden group-hover:block ml-1 text-red-500 hover:text-red-400"><X size={10}/></button>
                        </span>
                    ))}
                    {character.status.immunities.map(i => (
                        <span key={i} className="group relative px-2 py-1 bg-energia/10 text-energia rounded border border-energia/30 capitalize text-xs font-bold shadow-sm flex items-center gap-1">
                             Imunidade à {i}
                            <button onClick={() => removeResistance(i, true)} className="hidden group-hover:block ml-1 text-red-500 hover:text-red-400"><X size={10}/></button>
                        </span>
                    ))}
                </div>
             </div>
          </div>
          <ConditionsCard character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} />
        </div>

        <div className="lg:col-span-8 space-y-6">
          <div className="flex bg-eden-800 p-1.5 rounded-xl border border-eden-700 overflow-x-auto">
             <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('skills')} className={`flex-grow py-2 px-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap transition-all ${activeTab === 'skills' ? 'bg-eden-900 text-white shadow-sm border border-eden-600' : 'text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-700/50'}`}><Dice5 size={16} /> Perícias</button>
             <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('inventory')} className={`flex-grow py-2 px-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap transition-all ${activeTab === 'inventory' ? 'bg-eden-900 text-white shadow-sm border border-eden-600' : 'text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-700/50'}`}><Backpack size={16} /> Inventário</button>
             <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('rituals')} className={`flex-grow py-2 px-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap transition-all ${activeTab === 'rituals' ? 'bg-eden-900 text-white shadow-sm border border-eden-600' : 'text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-700/50'}`}><BookOpen size={16} /> Rituais</button>
             <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('combat')} className={`flex-grow py-2 px-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap transition-all ${activeTab === 'combat' ? 'bg-eden-900 text-white shadow-sm border border-eden-600' : 'text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-700/50'}`}><Swords size={16} /> Combate</button>
             <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('description')} className={`flex-grow py-2 px-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap transition-all ${activeTab === 'description' ? 'bg-eden-900 text-white shadow-sm border border-eden-600' : 'text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-700/50'}`}><User size={16} /> Descrição</button>
             <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('team')} className={`flex-grow py-2 px-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap transition-all ${activeTab === 'team' ? 'bg-eden-900 text-white shadow-sm border border-eden-600' : 'text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-700/50'}`}><Users size={16} /> Equipe</button>
             <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('abilities')} className={`flex-grow py-2 px-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap transition-all ${activeTab === 'abilities' ? 'bg-eden-900 text-white shadow-sm border border-eden-600' : 'text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-700/50'}`}><Zap size={16} /> Habilidades</button>
             <button onClick={() => setActiveTab('notes')} className={`flex-grow py-2 px-3 rounded-lg text-sm font-bold flex items-center justify-center gap-2 whitespace-nowrap transition-all ${activeTab === 'notes' ? 'bg-eden-900 text-white shadow-sm border border-eden-600' : 'text-eden-100/50 hover:bg-eden-700/50'}`}><PenTool size={16} /> Anotações</button>
          </div>

          <div className="bg-eden-800 border border-eden-700 p-6 rounded-xl min-h-[500px]">
             {activeTab === 'skills' && <SheetSkills character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} />}
             {activeTab === 'inventory' && <SheetInventory character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} />}
             {activeTab === 'rituals' && <SheetRituals character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} />}
             {activeTab === 'combat' && <SheetCombat character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} combatState={combatState} setCombatState={setCombatState} />}
             {activeTab === 'description' && <SheetDescription character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} />}
             {activeTab === 'team' && <SheetTeam character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} />}
             {activeTab === 'abilities' && <SheetAbilities character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} />}
             {activeTab === 'notes' && <SheetNotes character={character} onUpdate={handleUpdate} />}
          </div>
        </div>

      </main>

      {showResistModal && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/80 backdrop-blur-sm flex items-center justify-center z-[80] p-4">
            <div className="bg-eden-900 border border-eden-600 rounded-xl w-full max-w-md shadow-2xl animate-in zoom-in-95">
                <div className="p-4 border-b border-eden-700 flex justify-between items-center bg-eden-800/50">
                    <h3 className="font-bold text-eden-100">Adicionar Resistência</h3>
                    <button onClick={() => setShowResistModal(false)}><X size={20} className="text-eden-100/50 hover:text-eden-100"/></button>
                </div>
                
                <div className="p-6 space-y-4">
                    <div>
                        <label className="block text-xs text-eden-100/50 uppercase font-bold mb-2">Tipo de Dano</label>
                        <select value={selectedDmgType} onChange={(e) => setSelectedDmgType(e.target.value)} className={INPUT_STYLE} style={{ colorScheme: 'dark' }}>
                            {DAMAGE_TYPES_INFO.map(d => <option key={d.id} value={d.id}>{d.name}</option>)}
                        </select>
                        {selectedDmgData && <p className="mt-2 text-xs text-eden-100/60 bg-eden-950/50 p-2 rounded border border-eden-700/50 italic">{selectedDmgData.desc}</p>}
                    </div>
                    <div className="flex items-center justify-between bg-eden-950 p-3 rounded border border-eden-700">
                        <label className="flex items-center gap-2 text-sm text-eden-100 cursor-pointer">
                            <input type="checkbox" checked={isImmune} onChange={e => setIsImmune(e.target.checked)} className="accent-energia w-4 h-4" /> Imunidade Total
                        </label>
                        {!isImmune && (
                            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                                <span className="text-xs text-eden-100/50 font-bold uppercase">Valor</span>
                                <input type="number" value={resistValue} onChange={e => setResistValue(e.target.value)} className="w-16 bg-eden-900 text-eden-100 border border-eden-600 rounded p-1 text-center font-bold outline-none focus:border-energia" />
                            </div>
                        )}
                    </div>
                    <button onClick={handleAddResistance} className="w-full py-2 bg-energia text-eden-900 font-bold rounded hover:bg-yellow-400 transition-colors">Confirmar</button>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
      )}
      
      {showLevelUp && (
          <LevelUpModal 
              character={character} 
              targetNex={targetLevel}
              onConfirm={(updates) => {
                  handleUpdate(updates);
                  setShowLevelUp(false);
                  alert("NÍVEL AUMENTADO! Atualize seus PV/PE/SAN e verifique novos poderes.");
              }}
              onCancel={() => setShowLevelUp(false)}
          />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}



========================================
FILE: characterService.ts
PATH: D:\Programs\eden-arquivos\eden-arquivos\src\services\characterService.ts

import { db } from '../config/firebase';
import { collection, addDoc, serverTimestamp } from 'firebase/firestore';
import type { CharacterSheet } from '../types/characterSchema';

// Tabelas de PV/PE/SAN por Classe (NEX 5% Inicial)
const CLASS_STATS = {
  combatente: { pv: 20, pe: 2, san: 12, pvPerNex: 4, pePerNex: 2, sanPerNex: 3 },
  especialista: { pv: 16, pe: 3, san: 16, pvPerNex: 3, pePerNex: 3, sanPerNex: 4 },
  ocultista: { pv: 12, pe: 4, san: 20, pvPerNex: 2, pePerNex: 4, sanPerNex: 5 },
  mundano: { pv: 8, pe: 1, san: 8, pvPerNex: 0, pePerNex: 0, sanPerNex: 0 }
};

// Função auxiliar para remover campos undefined (Firestore odeia undefined)
const sanitizeObject = (obj: any): any => {
  // O JSON.stringify remove automaticamente chaves com valor undefined
  return JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(obj));
};

export const saveCharacter = async (characterData: CharacterSheet) => {
  try {
    // 1. Cálculos Finais de Status Base (NEX 5%)
    const cls = characterData.progression.class || 'mundano';
    // Fallback de segurança
    const stats = CLASS_STATS[cls as keyof typeof CLASS_STATS] || CLASS_STATS['mundano'];
    
    const vig = characterData.attributes.vig;
    const pre = characterData.attributes.pre;

    // Fórmulas do Livro Base para NEX 5%
    const maxPV = stats.pv + vig;
    const maxPE = stats.pe + pre;
    const maxSAN = stats.san;

    // 2. Limpeza dos dados (Remove undefined)
    const cleanCharacterData = sanitizeObject(characterData);

    // 3. Montagem do Objeto Final
    const finalData = {
      ...cleanCharacterData,
      status: {
        ...cleanCharacterData.status,
        pv: { ...cleanCharacterData.status.pv, max: maxPV, current: maxPV },
        pe: { ...cleanCharacterData.status.pe, max: maxPE, current: maxPE },
        san: { ...cleanCharacterData.status.san, max: maxSAN, current: maxSAN },
      },
      // Timestamps do servidor (não podem passar pelo sanitizeObject pois são objetos especiais)
      createdAt: serverTimestamp(),
      updatedAt: serverTimestamp(),
      userId: 'guest_user', 
    };

    // 4. Envio ao Firestore
    const docRef = await addDoc(collection(db, "characters"), finalData);
    console.log("Ficha salva com ID: ", docRef.id);
    return docRef.id;

  } catch (e) {
    console.error("ERRO CRÍTICO AO SALVAR: ", e);
    throw e; // Re-lança para o componente tratar
  }
};



========================================
FILE: characterSchema.ts
PATH: D:\Programs\eden-arquivos\eden-arquivos\src\types\characterSchema.ts

export type AttributeKey = 'agi' | 'for' | 'int' | 'pre' | 'vig';
export type SkillLevel = 'destreinado' | 'treinado' | 'veterano' | 'expert';
export type DamageType = 'balistico' | 'cortante' | 'impacto' | 'perfurante' | 'fogo' | 'frio' | 'eletricidade' | 'quimico' | 'morte' | 'sangue' | 'medo' | 'conhecimento' | 'energia' | 'mental';
export type NumericBonusType = string;

export interface TextObject {
  id: string;
  x: number;
  y: number;
  text: string;
  color: string;
  fontSize: number;
  // Campos adicionados para o editor avançado:
  align: 'left' | 'center' | 'right'; 
  width: number;
  height: number;
  borderColor?: string;
  backgroundColor?: string;
}

// NOVA INTERFACE PARA IMAGENS
export interface ImageObject {
  id: string;
  x: number;
  y: number;
  src: string; // Base64 da imagem
  width: number;
  height: number;
}

export interface NotePage {
  id: number;
  title?: string; // Adicionado título
  drawing: string;
  texts: TextObject[];
  images: ImageObject[];
}

export interface CustomEffect {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: 'bonus' | 'penalty' | 'other';
  target?: string; // PV, PE, SAN, Defesa...
  targetSubType?: string; // Atual, Máximo, Tipo de Dano...
  value?: string; // "+1d8", "5", "Resistência"
  description?: string;
}

export interface CustomAbility {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  type: 'active' | 'passive';
  description: string;
  cost?: number; // PE
  effects: CustomEffect[];
}

export interface ItemEffect {
    id: string; name: string; description: string; targetType?: string; element?: string; allowedTypes?: string[];
    bonuses?: { type: NumericBonusType, value: number | string, condition?: string }[];
    complexEffect?: string;
}

export interface InventoryItem {
    id: string; name: string; category: number; space: number;
    type: 'weapon' | 'protection' | 'general' | 'ammo' | 'amaldicoado' | 'accessory' | 'explosive' | 'paranormal';
    subType?: string; quantity: number; isEquipped: boolean;
    modifications: ItemEffect[]; curses: ItemEffect[]; damage?: string; details?: string;
}

export type TeamRole = 'tanque' | 'suporte' | 'curandeiro' | 'oportunista' | 'investigador' | 'terapeuta' | 'sabotador' | 'polivalente' | 'lobo_solitario'; 

export interface ActiveCondition {
  id: string; name: string; description: string; durationType: 'turnos' | 'cena' | 'indefinida'; durationValue?: number; effects?: { target: string, value: number }[];
}

export interface CharacterSheet {
  id: string; userId: string; createdAt: string; updatedAt: string; isPublic: boolean; version: string;

  info: {
    name: string; player: string; campaign: string; archetype: string; age: number; gender: string; portraitUrl: string; appearance: string; personality: string; history: string;
  };

  attributes: { agi: number; for: number; int: number; pre: number; vig: number; };

  notes: NotePage[];

  progression: {
    nex: number; patente: string; prestigePoints: number;
    class: 'combatente' | 'especialista' | 'ocultista' | 'mundano';
    origin: { id: string; name: string; }; trail: string;
    afiinity?: string | null;
    attributeIncreases?: Record<number, string>;
  };

  status: {
    pv: { current: number; max: number; temp: number; }; 
    pe: { current: number; max: number; temp: number; }; 
    san: { current: number; max: number; temp: number; }; 
    defense: { passiveMod: number; tempMod: number; };
    displacement: { baseMetres: number; tempMod: number; };
    resistances: Record<DamageType, number>; 
    immunities: DamageType[];
    conditions: ActiveCondition[];
    // NOVO: Array de IDs dos rituais sendo sustentados atualmente
    sustainedIds: string[]; 
  };

  skills: Record<string, { level: SkillLevel; isTrained: boolean; miscBonus: number; customName?: string; }>;

  inventory: { items: InventoryItem[]; weapons: any[]; creditLimit: string; maxLoad: number; };

  abilities: any[];
  rituals: any[]; // Aqui ficam os rituais aprendidos
  
  teamStrategy: {
    role: TeamRole; roleAbilities: Array<{ id: string; name: string; currentLevel: 0 | 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5; }>;
    favoriteFormations: string[]; isFormationActive: boolean;
    loneWolf: { isActive: boolean; extraPowersChosen: Array<{ nexSource: number; powerId: string; powerName: string; }>; };
  };

  classPowers: {
    coreLevel: number; // Nível do poder principal (0 a 3)
    selectedIds: string[]; // IDs de classPowers.ts
  };
  paranormalPowers: string[]; // IDs de paranormalPowers.ts
  customAbilities: CustomAbility[];

  combatLog: any[];
}

import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route } from 'react-router-dom';
import Home from './pages/Home';
import CreateSheet from './pages/CreateSheet';
import Sheet from './pages/Sheet'; // <--- Importe a nova página

function App() {
  return (
    <BrowserRouter>
      <Routes>
        <Route path="/" element={<Home />} />
        <Route path="/criar" element={<CreateSheet />} />
        {/* Rota Dinâmica: O ':id' vai pegar o código da ficha na URL */}
        <Route path="/ficha/:id" element={<Sheet />} />
      </Routes>
    </BrowserRouter>
  );
}

export default App;
